On the Eve of the Outbreak of the East African War: Fascist Party Conducts General Mobilization Exercises

High Tension Yesterday Afternoon Beginning at 3:30 PM; At a Signal, They Gather in the Square to Listen to the Prime Minister's Speech; Italian Troops Cross Border; Abyssinian Government Protests to League of Nations

(Rome) The long-awaited and repeatedly postponed general mobilization drill of national Fascist party members began today. This move is sufficient to show Italy's national unity in its war against Abyssinia. (2nd National Telegram)

(Rome) The general mobilization exercise of national Fascist groups is scheduled to be held at 3:30 PM today. It is generally believed that the military action in East Africa will begin after the implementation of this exercise. The Propaganda Department denied the claim that Italian troops had invaded the border of Abyssinia this afternoon. However, it is generally believed that the war is imminent. (2nd Havas Telegram)

(Rome) Today at exactly 3:30 PM, the national Fascist Party's test general mobilization signal was issued simultaneously across the country. The people's excitement reached its peak. The Rome authorities announced to the public that all churches would ring their bells at the same time, and the sirens would sound every three minutes to mobilize people. Upon the signal, all stores and factories, except for emergency public affairs, should immediately close their doors, and workers should rush home to put on their uniforms. By 5:30 PM, they must gather at the meeting place. An hour later, Mussolini will broadcast a speech from the balcony of the Palazzo Venezia to 15 million Fascist party members nationwide and may take the opportunity to announce the start of the African war. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) Fascist Party Secretary Starace broadcast a report on the wireless radio station at 2:20 PM, stating that the general mobilization exercise of national Fascist groups is scheduled to begin at 3:30 PM this afternoon. Loudspeakers have been installed in all cities, towns, streets, and alleys so that people across the country can listen to the Prime Minister's speech. In addition, the police have taken special measures to protect foreign embassies, and 10,000 police officers have been dispatched. The national army has remained in the barracks since this morning, awaiting orders. At 3:30 PM this afternoon, when the alarm signal is issued simultaneously across the country, the Fascist Party members of all Fascist Party groups will immediately gather at the designated locations. All stores should also strictly close their doors and windows. The weather is very bad today. It has been raining since morning and has not stopped. The rain is even heavier this afternoon. Fascist Party Secretary Starace is scheduled to report on the progress of the general mobilization exercise again at 5:30 PM this afternoon, before the Prime Minister's speech. (2nd Havas Telegram)

Important Meeting of the British Cabinet; All Ministers of National Defense Departments Attend

(London) The British Cabinet held two important meetings today, one in the morning and one in the afternoon. During the morning meeting, all cabinet members felt they needed to wait for developments in Geneva, but were prepared to hold an emergency meeting at any time. It was also heard that the administrative departments of national defense were given full authority to consult with Prime Minister Baldwin and adopt plans as required by the situation. In the afternoon, Prime Minister Baldwin met with the three ministers of the Navy, Army, and Air Force, as well as Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain, Foreign Secretary Hoare, President of the Board of Trade Runciman, Colonial Secretary MacDonald, and Home Secretary Simon to discuss everything. The chiefs of staff of the Air Force and Navy, as well as the permanent under-secretary of the Foreign Office, also attended the discussion. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Urgent Telegram from Addis Ababa: The Ethiopian government received reliable information that Italian troops had crossed the undefined border on the west side of Mount Moussa Ali, at the junction of Ethiopian, French Somaliland, and British Somaliland, and entered Ethiopian territory. However, hostilities have not yet broken out. Crown Prince Asfaw Wossen is currently taking steps to defend against the enemy. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

Addis Ababa: After receiving news of the Italian army's intrusion near Mount Moussa Ali, the Ethiopian government immediately lodged a protest with the League of Nations and requested that an investigative team be dispatched immediately to investigate the matter. It is now heard that if a definite statement of intent from Italy is not received, a general mobilization order will be announced tomorrow. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Addis Ababa: The Ethiopian Emperor today sent a telegram to the League of Nations, stating that the Italians are currently establishing military bases in Ethiopia, with the aim of launching a large-scale attack. The Council of the League of Nations should immediately send personnel to inspect, he said. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

(Geneva) The League of Nations has just received a telegram from the Emperor of Abyssinia reporting that Italian troops have invaded the country's borders and lodging a protest. (Havas dispatch, 2nd)

(Rome) The Foreign Ministry spokesman officially stated today that he was unaware of the news that Italian troops had crossed the Ethiopian border. However, he said that he deeply felt that the Ethiopians were unable to resist and would soon attack the Italian army. He also said that Ethiopia's provocative attitude might not only endanger Italian territories, but also the territories of other countries. (National Telegram, 1st)

(Rome) There were rumors that Italian troops stationed in East Africa had invaded the Ethiopian border. Officials here have just issued a public statement denying this claim. (Havas dispatch, 2nd)

Italian Army Prepares to Attack Ethiopia

Italian troops on the Eritrean front are ready to advance on Abyssinia from Eritrea. A special correspondent for the Associated Press, after inspecting 200 miles of the Italian front line by car, learned that an attack was possible within 72 hours. The movements of the front-line troops indicate that a large-scale offensive is prepared to be launched, but no officer knows when it will be launched. This morning, the reporter and Mussolini's son flew to the front line by plane. The area experienced was very extensive. Looking down from the plane, it was felt that the morale of the Italian soldiers was very high. They have received rigorous training and endured the various hardships of tropical warfare. The terrain, unfavorable for modern warfare, has been transformed by the Italian army. The wilderness can now be used for troop movement without difficulty. Military roads and military telegraph lines have been completely laid out. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Italian Consul in Ethiopia Ordered to Leave

Addis Ababa: With the Italo-Ethiopian war imminent, the Italian Embassy in Addis Ababa is now selling off everything, including all the furniture and carriages in the embassy, in preparation for leaving the country. Only six Italian nationals remain in the Ethiopian capital. Italy used to have six consulates in Ethiopia, four of which have already been closed, and the consuls have left Ethiopian territory. In addition, the consul stationed in Harar has also been ordered to leave, but the consul stationed in Adwa is temporarily staying in place awaiting orders. It is also heard that the Ethiopian consul stationed in Asmara, the capital of Italian Eritrea, has also been instructed to leave. (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Ethiopian Army Raises Spirits and Awaits Orders with Weapons at the Ready

Addis Ababa: A full mobilization order will be issued tonight. The Ethiopian Emperor has just instructed local authorities that this mobilization order is only a proclamation. When the mobilization order is issued, a religious prayer ceremony will be held in the palace. Civil and military officials, royal nobles, and journalists will all be present. At the same time, according to ancient Ethiopian customs, beacon fires will be lit on mountain tops everywhere to inform the public that war is approaching. (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Addis Ababa: The Ethiopian Emperor is still waiting for the opportune moment to issue his general mobilization order. According to sources here, the Ethiopian Emperor is still waiting for reports from Ethiopian envoy to France Heruy Wolde Sellassie and Ethiopian delegate to the League of Nations, the French national Qetché, both currently in Geneva. It is generally believed that war will break out after the mobilization order is issued, because it has become very difficult for tribal chiefs to restrain border troops. It is believed here that the Italian army is preparing to start military operations at Walwal, and launch a large-scale invasion of Ethiopia. Therefore, 25,000 Ethiopian troops are also prepared to resist Italian tanks and artillery with long guns and broadswords there. (National Telegram, 1st)

Italian Submarine Fleet Anchors in the Red Sea to Intercept Arms Shipments to Ethiopia

Ethiopian Authorities Take Preventive Measures; Many Arrested on Suspicion of Espionage

Addis Ababa: It is heard that 16 Italian submarines are currently anchored in the Red Sea in an attempt to intercept foreign ships carrying arms and war materials to Ethiopia. The Ethiopian authorities are also well aware of the activities of these individuals and have recently arrested many people suspected of being hostile to Ethiopia. The town of Jijiga has banned foreigners from entering. French authorities have now dispatched troops to guard the border to prevent the smuggling of arms. It is heard that there are currently two suspicious ships, without flags, cruising off the coast of French Somaliland. It is now believed that the ships are carrying thousands of machine guns intended to be delivered to the Ethiopian government. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Addis Ababa: It is heard that Ethiopian authorities will soon be able to import large quantities of arms, ammunition, and gas masks from various foreign countries. Fearing interception by Italian troops, they are taking various measures to prevent this. In the city of Jijiga, 50 kilometers from the border with Italian Somaliland, foreigners are prohibited from entering. Furthermore, several foreigners have been arrested on suspicion of espionage. The defense forces in the northern Ethiopian province of Gondar are commanded by the famous General Gassaa. It is heard that General Gassaa's son, Adal (name) Gassaa (surname), has assembled 20,000 soldiers and concentrated them in the Salale region north of the capital to strengthen the rear of the troops led by General Gassaa. Britain Reiterates Its Position; Does Not Want to Leave the League of Nations to Act Alone

League of Nations' Decision on Sanctions Must Meet Two Principles; Must Encircle All Powerful Countries in the World; Explains Difficulties Regarding Inability to Act Forcefully in the Sino-Japanese Case

(London) Official circles here today explained Britain's attitude toward the Italo-Ethiopian issue, stating that Britain does not want to leave the League of Nations to act alone. Britain has done its duty by supporting the League of Nations in the current crisis. Whether the Italo-Ethiopian dispute can be resolved quickly depends entirely on how other countries do their duty. If the League of Nations proves to be ineffective, the British public will inevitably cease to pay attention to the League of Nations. Therefore, to keep the mechanism for peaceful resolution of international disputes intact, all governments must actively support it unanimously. If the League of Nations decides on sanctions in the future, these measures must be consistent with the following two principles: (1) All powerful countries must be included; (2) They must not fail due to the actions of non-member states. The second point is especially important when implementing economic sanctions. In terms of phenomena, the United States will not hinder the actions of the League of Nations, and Germany will not act recklessly, dragging itself into the vortex of the dispute. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini recently stated that Britain knew of Italy's wishes in Ethiopia as early as January of this year, but it was not until Cabinet member Eden's visit to Rome in June that Britain explained its attitude. This statement is inaccurate. Since the Walwal incident last December, there has been hardly a week in which Britain has not clearly expressed its concern about Italian policy, and especially its impact on the collective security system. There is no reason to say that the British government allowed Italy to harbor illusions. Regarding future issues, although there is no hope that war can be avoided, Britain will obtain the best results from the League of Nations machinery to the extent of its power, so that the war ends as soon as possible. As for the criticism that Britain took no action regarding the Japanese invasion of Manchuria, while its attitude toward the Italo-Ethiopian dispute is tough, it must be understood that without the participation of Russia and the United States, the League of Nations could not take any action in Manchuria. But today, the League of Nations can actively handle the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, and there is no reason for Britain to adopt a policy of folding its arms and standing by. British officials also stated that the British government is not pursuing its policy for private gain. Britain has an obligation to protect Lake Tana on behalf of Egypt and Sudan, but Britain is unwilling to carry out the plan to build a dam on the lake, which shows that Britain is willing to put its own interests lightly, and to prioritize the general and more important needs of the League of Nations' policy. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

(London) It is learned that the British government has not only sought concrete expressions from France regarding the issue of sanctions, but has also made the same inquiry to other member states of the League of Nations. (National Telegram, 1st)

British Labour Party Congress Resolution; Advocates Imposing Sanctions on Italy

He believed that the armies of the British colonies should be placed under the League of Nations. This is not to say that the British colonies should no longer be protected by Britain. Germany, Austria, and Hungary Take the Opportunity to Revive the Idea of the Triple Alliance

Germany Proposes a Five-Year Non-Aggression Treaty to Austria; However, Berlin Believes That This Statement Has No Basis

(Vienna) According to reliable sources today, German Leader Hitler has instructed the German Ambassador to Austria, Papen, to propose to the Austrian government to conclude a five-year non-aggression treaty in advance. It is heard that if Austria is willing to conclude this treaty with Germany, then the German government is willing to make the following concessions: (1) Stop anti-Austrian government propaganda within Germany and Austria, and disband Austrian troops within Germany; (2) Germany will purchase more Austrian goods; (3) Cancel the 1,000 Mark blockade. At the same time, the German government requires the Austrian government to do the following: (1) Stop the anti-German attitude and participate in the alliance between Germany and Poland; (2) Stop the harsh policing laws imposed on National Socialist Party members within Austria; (3) Gradually release the National Socialist Party members imprisoned in detention centers. It is heard that the above plan has been agreed to by Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös and Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg. Gömbös's recent visit to Berlin is closely related to this matter. However, Austrian Deputy Prime Minister and Home Guard leader Starhemberg strongly opposes this proposal, because his power will be hit as a result. German Ambassador to Austria Papen is currently in Germany attending President Hindenburg's funeral. He will probably discuss everything with the Austrian Foreign Minister after returning to Vienna. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

(Berlin) Official circles here said that the statement that Germany asked the Austrian government to conclude a non-aggression treaty has no basis at all. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

France's First Post-War Battleship Launched

Fully Equipped to Deal with German Pocket Battleships

Lester: The first battleship built by France after the war, the "Dunkerque," with a displacement of 26,500 tons, will be launched today. This ship is the last word in France's response to the German pocket battleships in shipbuilding. This ship has a speed of 28.30 nautical miles and is equipped with eight 13-inch guns and sixteen 5.5-inch guns, while the German pocket battleships are only equipped with six 11-inch guns and eight 6-inch guns. This ship also has special equipment to defend against submarines and aerial attacks, and carries four Loire 130 seaplanes, with two launchers attached to launch the planes into the sky. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Moscow Newspaper Observes the Purpose of German-Hungarian Negotiations

To Create a Central European Power Bloc; Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös Returns Home from Berlin

(Moscow) "Pravda" commented on the Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös's visit to Germany, saying, "On the eve of the outbreak of military action in East Africa, Germany took the initiative to convene negotiations between Germany, Poland, and Hungary. This is sufficient to explain the purpose of these negotiations. German imperialism hopes that when Italy is tied down by Abyssinia and Britain's attention is also focused on East Africa, it can find a way to consolidate its position in Central Europe. Its first move is to solve the Austrian question. To accomplish this goal, it must form a power bloc to threaten the Little Entente countries (especially Czechoslovakia). This issue is the topic of the Berlin negotiations. The creation of the German-Polish-Hungarian bloc is the starting point for destroying the Little Entente countries. Gömbös's trip to Berlin and the German-Polish-Hungarian negotiations tell people that the fascist forces are trying to undermine European peace and create a new military bloc to re-divide Europe." Relocated to the Tannenberg Memorial; Hitler Attends in Person

Königsberg: Today, the Swastika flag is flying at half-mast throughout Germany, because President Hindenburg's remains are being relocated to the Hindenburg Tower in the Tannenberg Memorial. Naval Issues: Differing Opinions Within the British Government

Expanding the Navy vs. Awaiting Negotiations: Reply to Japan's Note on Naval Agreement

(London) British naval expert Mr. Horder recently published an article in the Daily Telegraph, detailing various differing views among government officials regarding naval policy. He stated that official opinions can be divided into two factions. One faction advocates immediately strengthening naval armaments, replacing all old ships that have reached the end of their service life, and building new ships. The other faction opposes immediately expanding the navy, arguing that it would risk triggering a naval arms race between Britain, the United States, and Japan. Reportedly, when US President Roosevelt departed for the Pacific coast on September 29, he delivered a speech outlining the US government's naval policy, which seemed to issue a warning to Britain, stating that Britain should bear the responsibility for the consequences that would arise after the abolition of the London and Washington Naval Treaties. The faction in Britain advocating for the construction of new ships is using Roosevelt's speech as their basis and insisting that Britain must act quickly to avoid future problems. Regarding this matter, although the government has already approved a large-scale shipbuilding program, the specific details of shipbuilding will be determined after the UK has obtained results from naval talks with other related countries. (Havas Dispatch, 2nd)

(Tokyo) The Foreign and Navy Ministries have reached an agreement on the Japanese government's response to the British government's notification regarding the disarmament conference. The result is a decision to express that Japan's disarmament policy remains unchanged and to reiterate that Japan's policy is aimed at developing a navy that does not threaten or invade, and to request that the British authorities consider this. The response is currently being drafted by the Foreign Ministry and will be submitted to a Cabinet meeting on the 4th. After formal approval, it will be telegraphed to the acting ambassador in the UK for a verbal reply to the British Foreign Office. The content is reportedly as follows:

(1) Japan's disarmament policy has already been explained during the preparatory negotiations last autumn and in the memorandum of August 21. The content is fixed and cannot be reconsidered. In order to implement disarmament in practice, the Japanese government advocates abolishing all forms of the ratio system to establish equal armaments.

(2) If Britain recognizes this fundamental policy, Japan is prepared to participate in the conference. However, both quantitative and qualitative restrictions should be implemented simultaneously because implementing qualitative restrictions alone favors the major naval powers, which Japan absolutely opposes. (United Press Dispatch, 2nd)

(Tokyo) It is reported that the Foreign Ministry has begun consultations with the Navy Ministry regarding the suggestion from Britain to convene a naval conference. However, Japan's naval policy has already been decided by the Cabinet, so the results of the discussion do not need to be submitted to the Cabinet. What Japan wants is genuine disarmament, the abolition of offensive weapons, including battleships and aircraft carriers. (Reuters Dispatch, 2nd)

British Chancellor Announces: Huge Military Spending

Little Surplus Expected in Annual Revenue: Currency Stabilization Also Difficult to Consider

(London) Chancellor of the Exchequer Neville Chamberlain warned the audience in a speech at a bankers' banquet last night that although tax revenues have been strong recently, there may not be a large surplus at the end of the year, as optimists have predicted. The Chancellor said that the increase in expenditures in the past six months has exceeded his expectations by approximately 10 million pounds, and the funds currently used to increase national defense are not yet included. The tax revenue surplus must be offset by this. At a time when the recovery process seems to be making real progress in most parts of the world, recent developments in foreign affairs have opened up new sources of concern, which he must address. The Chancellor then mentioned the gold standard, saying that restoring the gold standard would prevent Britain from using its price stabilization and cheap money policies to suit its domestic needs, and further declines in prices would be even more harmful to the dominions and colonies. He meant that the time when we could risk sitting idly by has not yet arrived. We must be patient a little longer until the international sky is clearer and the situation is more stable, and the dollar and franc no longer glare at each other. (Reuters Dispatch, 2nd)

(London) Chancellor of the Exchequer Neville Chamberlain, speaking today at the International Chamber of Commerce conference in the House of Lords, declared that due to the current European political situation, discussions on international currency stabilization are difficult to consider for the time being, and even preliminary tests cannot be carried out. Although Chancellor Chamberlain hopes that a global currency agreement may be discussed in the future and that the gold standard may eventually be restored, the current situation is very unfavorable for this difficult test. (National Telegraph Dispatch, 1st)

US Department of Commerce Announces: Far East Trade Statistics: Increased Imports of Goods from Our Country

(Washington) The Department of Commerce today released its monthly report on Far East trade statistics, stating that imports of goods from various Far Eastern countries to the United States have increased, but exports of goods to China have decreased significantly. US imports from Asia in August totaled $48,619,000, compared to $33,137,000 during the same period in 1934. Imports from China totaled $5,087,000, compared to $2,478,000 a year ago. US imports from Japan totaled $12,633,000, compared to $9,103,000 in April of this year. Imports of goods from the Dutch East Indies totaled $4,573,000, compared to $3,341,000 during the same period last year. Imports from the Philippines to the United States increased sharply, reaching $7,987,000 in August of this year, compared to only $2,646,000 in August of last year. US exports to Asia totaled $24,398,000, compared to $32,005,000 a year ago. Exports to China totaled $1,740,000, compared to $6,030,000 during the same period last year. Imports from the US to Japan totaled $11,680,000, less than the $13,857,000 in August of last year. Exports to the Philippines totaled $3,450,000, compared to $4,545,000 in August of last year. (National Telegraph Dispatch, 1st)

US Silver Senators Dissatisfied with Silver Purchase Plan

Demand Silver as Currency

(Washington) Senator Thomas, leader of the US silver senators, announced today that if the government has no intention of immediately making silver the basic currency, they will demand the adoption of currency management similar to that of the United Kingdom. This statement aims to prompt the government to change its silver policy, arguing that purchasing silver is meaningless if it has no use. Thomas also strongly criticized the Treasury Department's silver policy, accusing it of buying silver at extremely low prices and only willing to raise silver prices to prevent the collapse of the silver market. He went on to say that there is currently no guarantee that the government will continue to purchase silver. If silver purchases are abandoned, the current silver policy will cause significant losses to the government and mine owners. Thomas stated that a rift has emerged in the Senate and House of Representatives regarding the silver issue, saying that representatives from silver-producing states seem satisfied with the government, but he is not. "We will not stop until silver is coined at $1.29 per ounce. Otherwise, we would rather abandon the current plan and seek other methods." (National Telegraph Dispatch, 1st)

International Commercial Telegram

—Reuters Special Commercial Telegram, October 2nd— Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today is 141 shillings and 10 pence, up 2.5 pence.

London Silver Market: Spot price unchanged, remaining at 29 and 3/8 pence. Futures rose 0.0625 to 29 and 7/16 pence. Chinese buying and selling were mixed, and speculators sold off. The closing market was stable.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was $4.9025, down 0.0125. After the first hour, it rebounded 0.0625, then fell 0.04375 at 2 PM to $4.89875.

British-French: The opening fell by 3 pounds to 74 francs and 40 centimes, then rose by 1 pound. At 1 PM in the afternoon, it fell by 3 pounds to 74 francs and 38 centimes, and then remained unchanged.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: The opening this morning fell by 2 points due to increased hedging. The market was stable, and prices rose before noon.

Chicago Wheat: The opening rose by 0.375, following Liverpool and Argentina. Wheat prices continued to rise before noon. Coarse grains opened down 0.125, but then rebounded. The market was quiet.

Liverpool Wheat: Due to a lack of short covering and good foreign telegrams, the opening rose this morning. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the December contract rose by 2 pence to 6 shillings and 6 and 7/8 pence.

Liverpool Cotton: Firm this morning. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the January contract price was 5.95, up 11 points.

Rubber

London: The opening was slightly loose. The trading price for the January-March contract was 5 and 13/16 pence, down 0.0625 from yesterday's close. Although the market gradually stabilized before noon, prices did not change.

New York: Due to the fall in London prices today, the opening plummeted by 14 points. Trading was relatively active.

Securities

New Organization Implemented in Various County Governments in Fujian

(Xiamen) Provincial news: The provincial government will implement a new organization for various county governments starting on the 1st. All county education, construction, and road construction associations will be abolished. In counties that have been divided into districts, police agencies, regardless of whether they are bureaus, sections, police teams, or police stations, will be abolished. Police soldiers will be strictly selected and eliminated by the county magistrate. In counties that have not been divided into districts, police stations will also be reorganized. The original police equipment will be retained, and police officers will be removed, with management transferred to police assistants. (2nd, Special Dispatch)

Guangdong Province Reorganizes Finance

Reorganization of the Board of Directors of the Municipal Bank: Provincial Bank Supplements Paper Money Fund

Guangzhou communication: The Guangdong provincial government's financial institutions have historically included the Guangdong Provincial Bank and the Guangzhou Municipal Bank. The Provincial Bank has a larger scope, while the Municipal Bank is limited to the Guangzhou urban area. The Municipal Bank issues approximately 600,000 yuan in paper money. At the beginning of the month, the bank's board of directors was ordered to reorganize, adding three directors from the Provincial Bank to form a new board of directors. The Provincial Bank's board of directors has dispatched Chen Yue, Huo Baochai, and He Shaoqiong, while the Municipal Bank has dispatched directors Liu Binggang and Li Luchao to form the new board of directors. Chen Yue was publicly elected as the standing director, and it was decided to hold regular meetings twice a month. The detailed rules of the board of directors have been drafted by Chen Yue. The business operations of the Municipal Bank will generally remain unchanged, but the amount of paper money issued by the Municipal Bank is limited to 3 million yuan. The Provincial Bank and the Municipal Bank will exchange paper money without regional restrictions. It is said that this joint effort between the Provincial Bank and the Municipal Bank is purely to circulate the provincial and municipal finance and increase financial strength. As for the Provincial Bank, the Department of Finance previously approved the imposition of a 20% surcharge on nine types of taxes (namely, special tax on foreign paper, cattle hide tax, cattle slaughter tax, sugar tax, special tax on wax, paper money and ghost money tax, pig slaughter tax, surcharges on various counties, miscellaneous special tax on imported agricultural products, etc.) to guarantee the issuance of provincial silver notes. The collection period was set for one year, starting from April 15th of last year. April 14th of this year was the expiration date. Within one year, the revenue from this 20% surcharge was only over 3.47 million yuan, which was significantly different from the original estimated amount. It was then approved to extend the collection of the surcharge for another six months, from April 16th of this year to October 14th of this year. Now, the expiration date of October 14th is approaching rapidly, but the tax revenue collected is only over 1.6 million yuan, which is still insufficient to meet the original tax amount. The Supervisory Committee for the Issuance of Paper Money of the Provincial Bank, after considering the situation, believes that it is necessary to extend the collection of the surcharge again. It was then decided to extend the collection of the surcharge for the second time for six months, until April 15th of the 25th year of the Republic of China, until the original guaranteed amount of paper money issuance is fully collected, and then the collection will be stopped. The case of the second extension of the collection of the 20% surcharge on nine types of taxes was sent to the Department of Finance yesterday for submission to the provincial government for review and implementation.

The Wan Gong River Bursts: Hai and Su Counties Suffer a Great Calamity Together

The Town of Tanggou Sinks, Cries Echo Through the Fields: Two County Magistrates Have Submitted Their Resignations Taking Responsibility

Ba Jiang News: Recently, although the water situation in northern Jiangsu has gradually stabilized in the upper reaches, the flow in the lower reaches continues to increase. Rivers such as the Zhongyun, Liutang, Chaimi, and Shaoxiang have successively burst, and Donghai, Guanyun, Siyang, and Shuyang counties have suffered a great calamity together. Yesterday, a friend came to this town from Hai and Su counties, according to the report from Xuhai, the water situation is roughly as follows. The Yellow River breach is currently undergoing surveying work, but the blocking project has not yet been rushed to completion. However, its flow is extremely small, and the water level of Weishan Lake has also returned to normal, so the water situation in the upper reaches has stabilized. However, the lower reaches continue to rise. On the morning of the 27th, the right bank of the Wan Gong River in Shuyang, opposite Dashi Zhuang, burst, and the water poured towards Tanggou, with great momentum. In less than three li, the Dinggou water was blocked by the transverse weir built by Guanyun, and the accumulated ground water gradually rose. Residents are already surrounded by water, unable to escape. At that time, Guanyun troops were lined up on the opposite bank. At 8 PM, the levee near the Ma Hong area of Tangshan on the left bank suddenly tore, and at the same time, the levee on the opposite bank burst, and the water rushed into the river, and the water head suddenly rose by more than ten feet. At this time, the two county magistrates of Hai and Liu counties supervised the people and the law, and more than 1,500 people rescued them, but the people were discouraged because the opposite bank was breached, and the people's hearts were scattered. The two county magistrates, seeing this situation, were very anxious, and wept and persuaded the people, explaining the great righteousness of resisting the water. It was still in progress, and suddenly the opposite bank opened fire, and the work was frightened and escaped without a trace. However, the two county magistrates of Hai and Liu counties still could not bear to give up and negotiated with the opposite bank to stop the shooting, but no one answered. As a result, more than 500 people were gathered again from the six large and small lakes to rescue them for the second time, but 200 meters away from the construction site, more than 20 zhang were breached again, and it was impossible not to give up. As a result, Tanggou sank, half of Shuyang, and the sound of crying echoed through the fields. Now I heard that the county magistrates of Liuyang and Donghai believe that although this disaster was caused by artificial reasons, they are willing to take the blame and resign, and report to the provincial government to the effect that they are doing the right thing to the local area. In addition, according to news from the Department of Construction, the department attaches great importance to the breach of the Wan Gong River, and has sent water conservancy engineer Guan Fuquan and technician Xu Minghe to the Yishu tail area to inspect the flood prevention situation. Regarding the misunderstanding between Hai and Liu counties and Guanyun County due to flood prevention, Hai and Liu said that the breach of Liuguan Chaimi was caused by Guanyun building a dam in the Liuli River. Xu, the magistrate of Guanyun, said that the construction of the dam in the Liuli River was not related to the breach of the Chaimi River, and has telegraphed the province to report the situation of the dam construction and requested that personnel be sent to investigate to clarify the responsibility. The provincial department plans to find a proper way to first resolve the misunderstanding between the two parties and work hard on the embankment to avoid the expansion of the disaster area, and will send personnel to inspect if necessary. (October 1st)

Suzhou: The Small Loan Office Will Be Established

The Wuxian Small Loan Office, initiated by the Suzhou Jin Cheng Bank, has been agreed upon with the local government. Jin Cheng will allocate 80,000 yuan, the Wuxian Property Office will allocate 20,000 yuan, the Relief Institute will allocate 10,000 yuan, the Warehouse Association will allocate 5,000 yuan, and the County Chamber of Commerce will allocate 5,000 yuan, for a total of 120,000 yuan. Wu Yunzhai, the manager of the Jin Cheng Head Office, came to Suzhou on the 2nd to sign a contract and establish a board of directors and supervisors. The directors are Wu Qiyun, Zhang Hanwei, and others, five in total. The supervisors are Zhang Yipeng and Cheng Ganqing, two in total. It is scheduled to be officially established on Double Ten Day to start lending. The scope of lending will range from 10 yuan to 200 yuan, with a monthly interest rate of 9%, with the aim of supporting small businesses.

Wuxi: The Zhenxin Yarn Factory is Transferred for Takeover

The Zhenxin Yarn Factory incident outside the West Gate was handled impartially by the provincial party department last month and was resolved. All workers' saved wages, savings, and subsidies were paid out by the factory yesterday under the supervision of the party, government, and chamber of commerce. The salaries of the factory's employees have also been sent to the chamber of commerce by the factory for safekeeping. After the mediator, Mr. Xue Mingjian, agrees on the distribution procedures, a conclusion can be announced within days. Jiang Zeqing, the manager of the factory, has been ill for a long time and has expressed a passive attitude towards the factory's affairs, so he has firmly decided to resign. Now, a well-known yarn industry magnate adjacent to the factory, seeing that the Zhenxin yarn and cloth factories are fully equipped and that it is a pity that they have been shut down, and that many workers have lost their jobs, and that the future of the yarn market is stable, has proposed to invest in taking over the factory. He has been actively working in Shanghai in recent days and has obtained the consent of the Shanghai Bank, and it will soon become a reality.

Changzhou: Bizarre Corpse Crushed by Train

Xu Dezhe, the patrolman of the Fourth Police Station outside the East Gate of the Wuyi Public Security First Branch, was ordered to patrol along the railway at around 5 PM on the 1st. Near the 136-kilometer telegraph pole near Dingyan, he saw an unidentified male corpse. The corpse was naked, without a thread of clothing, and appeared to be about 30 years old. The right little foot was broken, and the right back was injured and bleeding. It was observed that it was crushed by the train from Shanghai to Beijing at around 4:30 PM. He immediately ordered Zhen Ding to guard the corpse and reported to the First Branch and then to the local prosecutor's office to send personnel to verify the incident. However, the corpse was naked and the circumstances were bizarre. There are currently no relatives claiming the body, and it is impossible to determine whether it was crushed to death or murdered.

Ning: Arrested Criminal Who Robbed the Shanghai Post Office

The Shanghai Post Office was robbed of a large sum of money, and a bodyguard was shot and killed by the bandits. Several suspects were arrested in Shanghai and confessed that their accomplice, Monk Huicheng, had fled to Guanyin Pavilion in Funing, Jiangbei. On the 29th, Liang Yuliang, a detective from the Public Concession Police Department, and Bao Deshou, an investigator, came to Fu with informants Chen Changyu and Tian Changfu (both natives of this county) to find out the whereabouts of the monk. At 8 AM on the 30th, they went to Guanyin Pavilion and arrested the monk. He was sent to the Guanyin County Government for detention. After interrogation, the monk confessed that his secular surname was Ji, his monastic name was Huicheng, his alias was Miaokong, and his nickname was Wukong. He was 38 years old and currently resided in Zhuoxian Temple in the Eighth District of this county. He went to Shanghai in 1933 and returned to Fu on July 21st of this year. In June of last year, he lived in the Dongyue Xiayuan Temple on Datong Road in Shanghai. I became a monk when I was a child. I was arrested by the Public Security Bureau in Shanghai for privately trading in military supplies and sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment, etc. Fifteen yuan in banknotes, a white silk handkerchief, and two silver yuan were found on his body, as well as an invoice. The detective Liang Yuliang requested that the money and items be preserved together and telegraphed Shanghai to prepare documents to bring him back to Shanghai for trial.

Local News

Minister Kong Speaks on the Current Financial Situation: Major Banks Will Absolutely Not Be Shaken. He Hopes the People of the Country Will Not Lightly Believe in Baseless Rumors.

The Central News Agency reporter met with Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan, Minister of Finance, and President of the Central Bank, and asked about the government's measures regarding the current social, economic, and financial situation. He said: Since the economic recession has affected our country, industry and commerce have gradually declined, and the market situation has deteriorated. Moreover, due to the financial community's caution and conservatism caused by various rumors, they have been very careful about loans. The market has become stagnant day by day. For the past year, the Ministry of Finance, due to its responsibilities, has been trying its best to provide relief. People's hearts have begun to stabilize, and the market has gradually stabilized. According to reports from the responsible departments, exports have increased sharply recently, and except for the flood-affected counties, all regions have celebrated a good harvest. The social economy should become more active day by day. However, recently, there have been people who do not understand the truth, who have listened to unscrupulous elements, who have fabricated various rumors about the banks for their own selfish purposes. This has led to the spread of false information and disrupted the market. This not only confuses public opinion but also violates the law. It should be known that banks with well-known reputations have a long history and a solid foundation in serving society and consolidating finance, and will absolutely not be shaken. Moreover, in order to consolidate the national economy and protect the people's savings, the government must also provide strong assistance as its backing. The rumors fabricated by traitors are entirely malicious. I hope that the people of our country will not lightly believe them. The slanderous schemes of the rumor-mongers will only disturb and harm themselves.

Money Trade Association, Held Representative Congress Yesterday

He Zhongxiao and Eight Others Elected as New Executive Committee Members, Sworn into Office, First Meeting Scheduled

The Shanghai Money Trade Association held its second provisional representative congress at 2 p.m. yesterday at its Ningbo Road location. A total of 184 member representatives were present, including Li Shoushan, Yun Qing, Shao Yanshan, Xi Jiming, Zhang Mengzhou, Chen Lishan, Chen Shengwu, Sheng Xiaoshan, Liu Wuqiao, Qian Yuansheng, Yan Dayou, Zheng Bingquan, Feng Yigui, Feng Meiqing, Chen Songquan, Xie Tianbao, Zhao Zifeng, Ye Xiuchun, Sheng Mengli, Chen Hongqing, Gu Xueqing, Zheng Boren, Zhao Songyuan, Chen Runjin, Zhang Dafu, Qi Ziquan, Feng Zexuan, Shen Liangliang, Wang Jiemei, Yao Deyi, Xu Shanchang, Wang Zhongshu, Hu Chunxiang, Qin Zhenfu, Xu Wenqing, Shen Jiuyu, and 154 others. The Municipal Party Headquarters sent Zhu Yakui, the Social Affairs Bureau sent Song Zhongqing, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent Luo Qinghua to attend for supervision and guidance. Qin Qiqing, manager of the Money Trade Preparation Bank, was also present as an observer.

Chairman's Report

The congress began with Chairman Qin Runqing presiding and Ge Huaiqing taking minutes. After the formalities, the chairman reported, saying that today marks the second re-election period for the association. It is an honor to have representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Social Affairs Bureau, and Municipal Chamber of Commerce present to supervise the election and provide guidance. Since the first re-election on October 2, 1933, it has been exactly two years today, and a re-election is required according to the regulations. Since Runqing and others were entrusted with the responsibility of committee members due to the misplaced affection of fellow traders, they have served during a period of economic decline, and they feel deeply ashamed for having achieved little and failed to live up to the expectations of their fellow traders. Moreover, in the past two years, the financial turmoil has surged, and our industry has been at the forefront, facing storms and crises. Faced with this dangerous situation, the committee members have been deeply concerned and have worked tirelessly to strengthen the industry itself and to cope with the changing environment. Fortunately, with the support of the authorities and the supervision of fellow traders, although there have been some setbacks, the overall situation has not been affected. The twists and turns of this process are appreciated by all traders. We are all in the same boat, and future troubles are far from over. Coping with everything in the future will be even more difficult than it is now. From now on, if our industry wants to stand firm and remain invincible, we must adapt to the trend, gradually innovate all facilities, maintain a prudent business policy, and strengthen unity among traders. By doing so, we can avoid being eliminated by natural selection and promote our industry. Now that the representatives present have reached the legal quorum, I hereby announce the opening of the meeting and respectfully listen to the instructions of the superiors, which will be of great benefit to us.

Party and Government Instructions

(1) Zhu Yakui of the Municipal Party Headquarters stated that today he represents the Municipal Party Headquarters to participate in the representative congress of your association. The punctual arrival of everyone sufficiently demonstrates the admirable spirit of your association. Your association's election has been held for two years, during which the market has undergone drastic changes. Qianzhuang have a long history and, like the Banking Association, are part of the same financial group, closely related to industry and commerce. Since the financial panic last year, the market has been extremely depressed. How to work hard to restore the economy is the urgent task for the future. However, China is an agricultural country, and farmers account for more than 80% of the population. Therefore, to revive the market, it is first necessary to revive the countryside and increase purchasing power. The rampant bandits in the interior are also the reason for the decline of the countryside. Assisting the rural economy and consolidating the rural foundation will make it easier to revive Shanghai and make the market prosperous. (2) Song Zhongqing of the Social Affairs Bureau said that today is the second re-election representative congress of your association. It is a great honor for me to participate. The Party representative has already detailed the relationship between your association and industry and commerce, so I will not repeat it. For thousands of years, our country used to barter, without currency as a medium. Later, it was found to be inconvenient, and substitutes were invented. Initially, shells were used, followed by currency. Silver and money are the medium of exchange. The credit of the qianzhuang industry is well-known and carries unlimited responsibility. Now that the market is so depressed and industry and commerce are extremely depressed, the silver and money industry bears the greatest responsibility. How to save people and save oneself is something that the leaders of the qianzhuang industry present should study together. (3) Luo Qinghua of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stated that today Qinghua represents the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to attend the second representative congress of your association. I am extremely honored to meet with the elders of the qianzhuang industry. Qinghua is also employed by the Silk Industry Bank, so indirectly, I can also be said to come and observe as a colleague. Because of the usual business relationship, it feels even more cordial to be together today. Therefore, I feel that what I want to contribute to your association should be straightforward and candid. People often refer to the qianzhuang and banking industries as the financial industry. According to the definition of finance, "jin" means currency and "rong" means circulation. Therefore, the business of the silver and money industry is to circulate the economy, and the principle is to grant and receive credit. In recent years, our country has suffered frequent natural and man-made disasters internally and has been hit by economic waves externally, resulting in the decline of all enterprises, the tightening of credit, and the extreme situation. Society is filled with a gloomy and uneasy atmosphere, and different opinions are rife, with no consensus. Some advocate currency expansion, repeating the mistakes of others, while others advocate bartering, returning to primitive life. In a declining world, rumors only serve to confuse people. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has conducted detailed research and believes that the current problem is not the lack of payment chips, but the exhaustion of credit chips. To correct this problem, it is necessary to establish a credit system. The qianzhuang industry is a historical financial organization in our country. Prosperous cities throughout the country, even remote towns, have qianzhuang establishments. Historically, they have been particularly cautious in granting and receiving credit because they are unlimited organizations, and most shareholders are wealthy, so society has faith in them. As for the Shanghai qianzhuang industry, because colleagues can unite and communicate with each other, the credit is even better. Qianzhuang drafts have always been regarded as cash by industry and commerce. On the one hand, the qianzhuang industry is more familiar with the credit investigation of the industrial and commercial sectors, sometimes surpassing any expert. Therefore, the credit loans of industry and commerce are mostly from the qianzhuang industry. Since our country has encountered an unprecedented economic crisis, the business of the qianzhuang industry has inevitably contracted. However, the world is suffering, and since we believe that only by establishing a credit system can we overcome the current economic difficulties, colleagues in the qianzhuang industry should continue to work hard based on their experience and not lightly shirk their responsibilities. In view of the establishment of a joint reserve by your association in recent years to increase the credit of colleagues, it is sufficient to prove the spirit of unity among colleagues, which is worthy of praise by the public. I hope to expand this scale and work together to deal with the current economic crisis, follow the meaning of human evolution, and improve business at any time to adapt to the modern environment, so that the colleagues of your association can carry forward and benefit the national economy. How could it be superficial?

Election Results

Wang Yangsu and Feng Yigui were appointed as vote counters, Zhang Dafu and Yuan Liwen as vote announcers, and Ge Huaiqing, Lu Jietu, and Xia Songsheng as ballot writers. The election results are as follows: (1) He Zhongxiao received 143 votes, Wang Jiemei received 130 votes, Xu Wenqing received 109 votes, Zhang Dafu received 104 votes, Lu Shuchen received 93 votes, Zhang Wenbo received 66 votes, Shen Jingliang received 60 votes, and Zhao Songyuan received 48 votes. The above eight people are the newly elected executive committee members. (2) Ye Xiuchun received 47 votes, Wu Zilin received 43 votes, Qin Zhenfu received 41 votes, Tian Zixin received 27 votes, and Zhang Shanlian received 27 votes. The above five people are alternate committee members. (3) The remaining committee members are Xi Jiming, Liu Wuqiao, Chen Lishan, Shao Yanshan, Yan Dayou, Zhang Mengzhou, Zheng Bingquan, and seven others. (4) The committee members whose terms have expired are Qin Runqing, Pei Yunqing, Yu Zuoting, Sheng Xiaoshan, Wang Huailian, Li Shoushan, Qian Yuansheng, Chen Shengwu, and eight others.

A temporary motion was made regarding the discount rate for September, and it was decided that it would be 95% discount in April. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe sanctions. I solemnly swear." Subsequently, representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce delivered brief speeches.

New Committee Thanks

Wang Jiemei, a newly elected executive committee member, gave a thank-you speech, saying, "Today is the swearing-in ceremony for the third-term elected executive committee members after the second re-election of our association. We are very honored to have representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to supervise the oath and give us instructions. We are ashamed of our lack of talent and burdened with this heavy responsibility, and we are deeply worried about failing. We can only encourage each other, abide by the oath, and the instructions of the oath supervisors, and strive to live up to the expectations of the representatives and the trust of the members of our association. We thank you on behalf of all the committee members." The meeting adjourned at 5 p.m., and it was decided to convene the first executive committee meeting within a few days to elect five standing committee members and then elect a chairman from among the committee members.

Resolution to Return Half of Relief Loans to Qianzhuang First

If Necessary, Loans May Still Be Borrowed

The Ministry of Finance's relief loan to qianzhuang is 25 million yuan, originally planned as 18 million yuan from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, 4 million yuan from various commercial banks, and 3 million yuan from the Money Trade Reserve. The lending and repayment methods are all handled as above. The commercial banks that borrowed the money have recently seen a great need for rural lending, and the local money market has gradually eased. They have written to the Shanghai Money Trade Supervision Committee to quickly instruct the various qianzhuang to repay the loans. According to the Xin Sheng She reporter, if the relief loans to qianzhuang are to be repaid in one lump sum, it is actually difficult to achieve. In order to take into account the interests of both lenders and borrowers, it was resolved that each qianzhuang should first repay a portion of the loan within the month, aiming to repay the full amount of 3 million yuan originally lent by the Money Trade Reserve, and repay half of the 4 million yuan lent by the various commercial banks. Repayments will continue in the future. However, if qianzhuang need to borrow money after repaying the loans, they may still borrow from the various commercial banks within the scope of the loans. It is said that the various commercial banks have agreed. The various qianzhuang have successively repaid the loans to the Central Bank, and a certain amount has already been accumulated. It is expected that the original plan to repay half of the loans lent by the various commercial banks can be repaid on schedule.

Insurance Department of the Central Trust Bureau, Started Business Yesterday

After the Central Trust Bureau started business on the 1st of this month, the Bureau followed the instructions of the National Government to establish an Insurance Department for the safety of public property and the protection of civil servants and soldiers, and for the benefit of society, to handle: (1) Fire insurance; (2) Marine insurance; (3) War and theft insurance; (4) Automobile insurance; (5) Life insurance; (6) All property and personal accident insurance, and reinsurance business. The Bureau allocated 5 million yuan of national currency as the independent fund of the Department, so the Department's accounting is independent and the funds are strong. From now on, the Chinese insurance industry will have this new force, and the reputation will be even more prominent. The Department officially started business yesterday.

Group Photo of the Economic Inspection Group to Japan

National Federation of Commerce Chairman Lin Kanghou Publishes "Observations on Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation"

Economic cooperation is not only necessary but essential, but obstacles to cooperation must be eliminated and prevented as much as possible. Sino-Japanese trade associations should be formed by both parties.

Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce, is scheduled to depart for Japan on the 6th of this month for an economic study tour. He has specially published an article on Sino-Japanese economic cooperation to draw the attention of the people of both countries. A reporter from the New Sound News Agency has specially sought to record the original text as follows: Before discussing this topic, I will quote Mencius's words: "Go out and enter as friends, watch and help each other, and support each other in sickness." I will also quote a Chinese proverb: "A golden neighbor is better than silver relatives." I will also quote a traditional Chinese motto: "Be kind to neighbors and treat them well." From the three items quoted above, we know how much the Chinese people value their neighbors. This is true for individuals, and it is also true for countries. Why is this so? It is because we want "economics" to be able to lift each other up and achieve mutual benefit. Economic support between Chinese rural villages: (1) Mutual labor assistance, for example, on a certain day, two people from household A go to household B to work, and on a subsequent day, two people from household B go to household A to work, called returning labor. This is assistance in terms of service. (2) Mutual borrowing of farm tools and mutual exchange of seeds. This is assistance in terms of materials. (3) Household A asks household B to plow the fields and remove weeds, and household B asks household A to thresh grain and grind it. This is assistance in terms of technology. The above three types of support are not due to coercion or threats, or based on one party's opinion, forcibly imposed. Therefore, the neighbors are very friendly to each other, and the scope of economic support is even broader, such as helping each other with weddings, funerals, and celebrations. If there is a shortage, they share what they have. From this, we can see that economic support is essential and indispensable to mankind. International economic assistance can be used as an analogy. But in fact, we have gained an experience, that is, for example, if someone, Mr. A, relies on his wealth and power to treat his neighbors, he either encroaches on their land, or interferes in their family affairs, or forces them to obey him, and is arrogant everywhere. Then the neighbor fears him like a tiger and avoids him like a cat. On the surface, it seems that he can do whatever he wants, but in reality, he will never get the neighbor's economic assistance. It is tolerable in peacetime, but it becomes very difficult in times of crisis. Some people think that Mr. A only needs to control the neighbor and use his power to make him submit, so that he has no choice but to engage in economic support. In fact, if there is no emotion and the interests are different, even between father and son, husband and wife, and brothers, no fruitful economic cooperation can occur. And if the people completely believe that the government's economic policy is unfavorable, it is difficult to implement. If Mr. A uses coercive means to seek economic assistance from his neighbors, the result will be like an adult helping a child, rather than economic cooperation between adults. Between China and Japan, in terms of geography, history, race, and culture, economic cooperation is not only necessary but essential. But if we calmly and quietly recall the past, grasp the present, and observe the future, are there any obstacles to Sino-Japanese economic cooperation? Considering the facts, I am afraid that both Chinese and Japanese people will find it difficult to deny that there are no such obstacles. Since there is such an obstacle, we should strive to remove it in order to achieve the purpose of economic cooperation under the meaning of the Mencius quotation mentioned earlier. In ancient times, Japan took China as its teacher. In modern times, China takes Japan as its teacher. But when Japan took China as its teacher, Japan did not lose its sovereignty, and only looked to China for orders. When China takes Japan as its teacher, it naturally does not want to lose its sovereignty, and only looks to Japan for orders. Even learning from a teacher should not be like this, let alone economic cooperation. Sino-Japanese economic cooperation is definitely not unnecessary but essential. This is a future fact that no one can deny. That is, when Chinese and Japanese people fully recognize that Sino-Japanese economic cooperation is inevitable, they will be able to find ways to eliminate the obstacles left over from the past and present as much as possible. The scope of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation includes service, technology, and materials. Within this scope, not only does China need help from Japan, but Japan also needs help from China. Therefore, the Sino-Japanese economic cooperation should first establish the following principles: (1) Recognizing the indispensability of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. (2) Eliminating all existing, future, or planned obstacles to Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. (3) Developing as much as possible the necessary emotional and instrumental elements to promote Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. As for the central structure of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, it should be divided into two aspects: one is the government, and the other is the people. But both must have a unified and fair policy. As for the steps, on the Chinese side, first, the national economic organizations should be united and integrated, and all industries should be built into three-dimensional systems. It is absolutely impossible to continue to be scattered and unrestrained, each acting on its own. Otherwise, the national economy cannot cooperate, how can it cooperate with foreign countries? Although this can be done by people automatically, the responsibility for supervision still lies with the government. The Chinese government should establish an economic policy, emphasizing agriculture and industry or suppressing commerce, depending on the needs of the facts, and set a five-year or ten-year plan. On the Japanese side, its economic organization is much more advanced than China's, but in developing its national economy too rapidly, it inevitably contains political means and the mistaken idea that advancement is easier. There are many past examples, which need not be repeated. If economic cooperation is desired, all political and military actions should be considered not only not easy to promote Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, but also sufficient to hinder Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. Although it may not immediately lead to a lose-lose situation, in the end, it will inevitably suffer the consequences. From the current world situation and the internal economic situation of China and Japan, it is difficult to escape this conclusion that we are extremely unwilling to have. The most important thing is that merchants from China and Japan who engage in mutual trade should first unite and have their own organizations. These Sino-Japanese organizations will act jointly. With this union, the separation between the Chinese and Japanese people can be avoided, and this organization can also potentially promote close relations between the Chinese and Japanese governments. In addition to the above-mentioned organizations, leaders of the Chinese and Japanese people should form two Sino-Japanese trade associations and unite with each other to determine the content and means of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, so that Sino-Japanese economic cooperation can move from words to reality. In short, the economies of China and Japan should be promoted under the spirit of equality and mutual respect. The result will be that the Chinese and Japanese people will deeply recognize the true meaning of "Go out and enter as friends, watch and help each other, and support each other in sickness," "A golden neighbor is better than silver relatives," and "Be kind to neighbors and treat them well," and look forward to the broad road of peaceful coexistence and co-prosperity.

Japanese Fishing Boats Invade Our Territorial Waters, Japanese Embassy Agrees to Take Action

Japanese fishing boats often cross the border to fish in the waters off Zhejiang Province, infringing upon our maritime rights. The Zhejiang Provincial Government has telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to protest to Japan. Now we have received a note from the Japanese Embassy stating that the Japanese authorities have always taken practical measures to crack down on Japanese fishing boats fishing in Chinese territorial waters, and will continue to use the same approach in the future. However, when the Chinese side protested this matter, it only mentioned a certain number of ships, which made it impossible to investigate. If such incidents are discovered in the future, the ship's name, port of registry, the name of the captain or person in charge, and other necessary information for the investigation should be provided in detail before action can be taken. The Provincial Government has forwarded this note to the special commissioners of Yin, Linhai, and Yongjia, the county magistrates of the coastal counties, and the Second Marine Police Brigade for their information.

The Red Swastika Society's Relief Efforts in Hanyang and Hanchuan

After the Yangtze River flood occurred, Wu Heguang, the chief captain of the Red Swastika Society, immediately formed a team led by Captain Ouyang Dulin to Wuhan for relief. Now we have received a report from the Shanghai General Office of the Association from the forward relief team, which is recorded as follows: On July 5, our team distributed medicines in the area of Wutai Gate, Wusheng Gate outside the Kai Zi Gate, and the Glass Factory and Jinbaisha River in Wuchang to rescue the sick and disaster-stricken people. On the 10th, we took a small steamer to Hanyang, landed at Caidian in the second district, hired two rowing boats, and entered the Yuanjia Zui Baba Embankment, Fubai Ma Jiudou Embankment, and Donghu and Xihu, all the way to Chenggong Mountain and Yaojia Cen. After starting ashore at Songlin Zui, we passed through Xia Siling in Yu Chen Township and Zhenkong Valley, and went straight to the Yong'an Fort Market Town in the seventh district of the county. Along the way, the embankments were breached, the houses were destroyed, and it was a vast expanse of water, indistinguishable from the sky. After on-the-spot investigation, there were 1,525 households in the seventh district who could not survive without relief, and only 306 households in the third district. We distributed 200 bags of soybeans (broad beans), 200 bags of soybeans to Laocheng Rao in Yong'an Fort, 374 bags of No. 5 flour to Jurushan, 28 bags of pot scrub rice, 27 bags of fried wheat flour, and 7 bags of soybeans. We distributed 265 bags of soybeans to Jinniushan Berlin Store in Banzhu. We also found that there were 2,036 households in Tongle, Taihong, and Shengxian Townships in the second district. We distributed 298 bags of soybeans. After the Hanyang relief was completed, Captain Ouyang and his staff took a boat from X溝 to Hanchuan. At that time, Hu Zhongcheng, the captain of the third team, had been sent to Hanchuan by this office, and the work was combined. It was found that after the levee break in the fourth, fifth, sixth and third districts of the county, the areas near the town were all turned into swamps. The first, third and second districts were less affected. It is estimated that there are more than 110,000 disaster victims in the entire county who cannot survive without relief. We often started the inspection and distribution from the sixth district, which was the most severely affected by the disaster. It is estimated that there were 3,701 households and 16,687 disaster victims of all sizes in the five townships of the County River, Shenling, Gezhen, Dunshan, and Anle in the district. According to the principle of disaster relief to save the dying but not the poor, a total of more than 1,700 bags of flour were distributed. Now the distribution in the sixth district has been gradually completed. The two captains, Ouyang and Hu, and their staff will go to the fourth and fifth districts for inspection and distribution. Because the disaster situation in the fifth district is no less than that in the sixth district, it is still necessary to cross the water to go to and from the villages. Once there are wind and waves, the rowing boats cannot be used. This is the biggest difficulty. Of all the 4,090 bags of flour transported to Hanchuan, more than 1,700 bags have been distributed in the sixth district, and the remaining 2,300 bags are not enough to distribute in the fourth and fifth districts. It is estimated that more than 600 bags still need to be purchased. A total of 4,700 bags of flour were distributed in the third district. As for the first, second, third and third districts, soybeans were completely distributed, totaling 1,200 bags. The relief efforts in the entire county can be declared completed in the near future. During this period of intense work, the number of team members is not enough to distribute. It is planned to transfer more experienced team members to participate in order to speed up the process. This is the situation of the recent handling of the Hanyang and Hanchuan relief efforts by this team.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Instructs on the Doubts About the Use of Stamp Tax

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent letters to the Chinese and Western Pharmacy and the Detai Glassware Company yesterday, instructing on the doubts about the use of stamp tax, which are recorded separately as follows:

Invoice Binding The Association replied to the Chinese and Western Pharmacy in a letter stating: Respected Sir, in response to your previous letter, asking whether the invoice for ordering goods from your pharmacy, which is bound into a book of five pages, should be affixed with stamps as one piece, etc., we have forwarded it to the Ministry of Finance for verification and replied to you in advance. Now, on the first day of this month, we received a reply from the Ministry of Finance in the Tax Letter No. 7290 stating: "We have carefully checked the winter telegram and its attachments. The invoice used by the Chinese and Western Pharmacy has a clear list of the main brand and a list of other brands. The list is also attached with a summary, which is bound as a copy. If the date of delivery, list number, and amount of goods and silver contained in each list are the same as those contained in the summary, and are delivered at the same time as the summary, it can be considered as one piece, and sufficient stamps should be affixed in the summary. Each list does not need to be stamped again. However, if there is only a list and no summary, each list should still be stamped separately in order to prevent trickery. You should immediately forward this to your subordinates for compliance." We have sent a letter for your record and reply, hoping that you will check and handle it accordingly.

Stamp Tax on Old Books The Association also replied to Detai Glassware Company in a letter stating: We received your letter on the first day of this month. We have learned that you are inquiring about the stamp tax on account books. Now we reply as follows: (1) For old account books that have not yet been used up, which have been stamped with one dime, and are still in use, they can be used until the end of the year. There is no need to add more stamps. (2) For old account books that have been used up by the end of August, which have been stamped with one dime, the situation is the same as above. There is no need to add more stamps. However, if the old book is used up by the end of August, and a new book is replaced on September 1, this new book must be stamped with two dimes, and its validity can only be calculated until the end of the year. If it is used continuously after the beginning of spring without replacing a new book, it must be stamped with another two dimes.

A Large-Scale Meteorological Observatory is Established in Shenjiamen, Dinghai

This year, typhoons have blown through the coastal areas of Zhejiang Province many times, hindering agriculture, forestry, and water conservancy, and devastating the fishing industry, which is extremely serious. Therefore, the Zhejiang Construction Department believes that meteorology is of great importance to people's livelihood, and meteorological work should be actively carried out. It has now been resolved to establish a fire-scale meteorological observatory in Shenjiamen, Dinghai, specializing in reporting daily weather, so as to benefit agriculture, forestry, water conservancy, aviation, fishing, commercial ships, and civilian ships. This matter will be carried out in cooperation with the Academia Sinica.

Since the city government and its affiliated bureaus have concentrated their offices in the city's central district, the need for telephones has become increasingly urgent. The internal equipment and layout are extremely neat and perfect, and it has been praised as a model telephone bureau. All equipment adopts an automatic system, and in April of this year, the underground pipeline manhole and other projects were completed. In May, the overhead pole lines were effectively organized to ensure proper functioning. Subsequently, the telephone service was enabled at midnight on May 25, which was very convenient for all agencies, schools, and citizens in the city. The bureau, considering that the general public has not fully understood the organization of automatic telephones and the usual method of use, has taken advantage of the current National Games to open the branch during the games period for public viewing. It is reported that the daily opening hours are set from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM.
