Taxpayers' Association Executive Committee Xu Xiaochu and Others Request Public Works Department to Economize Expenses: Market Decline Affects Tax Revenue, Advance Expense Reduction to Lighten Citizens' Burden

Executive Committee members of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Xu Xiaochu, Jin Zongcheng, Zheng Chengqing, Ma Shaoquan, Jin Runxiang, Sun Mingqi, Chen Ziming, Xu Guanqun, Su Jiaxing, Shen Tianxin, etc., jointly sent a letter yesterday to the Ratepayers' Association to forward to the Public Works Department, requesting advance expense reduction to avoid affecting the citizens' burden. The letter states: "We respectfully inform you that the impact of the recession has spread throughout the world, and Shanghai, which is known as the first commercial port in East Asia, has also been drawn into the whirlpool. The market is declining, commerce is withering, and financial institutions, such as banks and money shops, have been closing down and liquidating one after another. Companies and firms that have difficulty maintaining operations and cannot bear the heavy burden have gone bankrupt. Others have been sealed off by the courts for failing to pay rent. Under these extremely depressed circumstances, stores and shops that are still struggling to operate are only reducing staff and salaries to tighten expenses. Among the expenses of stores, rent is a major item. At this time of market downturn, the movement to reduce rents has reached a boiling point. The achievement of this movement is also inevitable. If the rent reduction movement succeeds, the Shanghai Municipal Council will be indirectly affected. The property tax collected by the Municipal Council is proportional to the rent. If the rent is reduced, the property tax will also be reduced accordingly. The source of the Municipal Council's administrative expenses depends on the tax revenue from businesses and residents within the district, which is the largest source of tax revenue for the bureau. According to the bureau's full-year budget for 1935, it reached over 11.8 million yuan. However, compared to the actual number collected from January to the end of June 1935, there was a shortfall of over 260,000 yuan. It is speculated that the situation in the second half of 1935 will be even worse, with more shops closing down and residents moving back to their hometowns due to the difficulty of living. The number of vacant houses will increase, and rent will be reduced even further. The reduction in property tax collected by the Municipal Council may be even greater than in the first half of the year. However, considering the administrative scope of the bureau, it seems that this has not been taken into account. Foreign staff often receive huge salaries, as well as various items such as exchange rates, rent, and education allowances. The public believes that the orchestra can be abolished, but due to the fondness of a few Westerners, they are willing to provide circumstantial evidence and misinterpretations to keep it in existence. The expenditure on this orchestra in the first half of 1935 reached over 125,000 yuan, which amounts to over 250,000 yuan for the whole year. Furthermore, out of the bureau's total tax revenue of over 25.2 million yuan, less than 5% is allocated to education expenses. This suggests that the bureau's regular expenses do not seem to be appropriate. We believe that the bureau should adopt the same attitude under the current state of recession in Shanghai, where the entire society is generally reducing staff, salaries, and expenses. Except for the need to maintain security within the district due to the increasing number of unemployed people and those who disregard the law, the police force's expenses cannot be excessively reduced. Other expenses should be scrutinized for savings, which would be a significant amount. This, along with the reserve for deferred taxes and shortfalls, is the bureau's current and essential task. Furthermore, the Shanghai Telephone Company disregards the market's downturn and the difficulties of commerce, and at this time, it is increasing the people's burden, stubbornly adhering to the provision of ensuring a 1% annual profit. It is determined to raise telephone fees, as if the people's opposition can be ignored, and the provision of an annual interest of 1% must be maintained. If the company could pay attention to internal expenses and slightly tighten unnecessary expenses in light of the market trend, we fear that not only would telephone rates not need to be raised, but also the so-called 1% annual interest would be guaranteed and even exceeded. However, it does not attempt to do this and focuses solely on the burden of telephone users within its sphere of influence. This is the same as the Municipal Council, which is not concerned about the shortfall in tax revenue and remains unmoved. Under these circumstances, we taxpayers and telephone users, upon considering the increasing burden in the future, find it difficult to remain silent. Therefore, we respectfully submit this to your esteemed association, requesting that you suggest to the Municipal Council and the Shanghai Telephone Company that they pay attention to implementing government reduction. This would not only be fortunate for taxpayers and telephone users but also beneficial to the future of the bureau and the company. This is addressed to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Shanghai Municipal Council."

(7) All the wedding participants bowed once to the officiant. Thirty-One Silk Mills in Shanghai Have Resumed Operations

Due to the resurgence in silk sales in Europe and the United States and the increase in prices, the number of silk mills resuming operations in Shanghai has continued to increase. Mutual Aid Society: Method Set for Electing Rickshaw Pullers' Representatives

Regarding the issue of electing rickshaw pullers' representatives to the Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society, according to the society's regulations, the election method must be approved by the Public Works Department's board of directors. The election method has now been drafted by the Mutual Aid Society's board of directors, slightly revised by the Public Works Department's Special Committee on Rickshaws, and then submitted to the Public Works Department's board of directors for approval. According to this method, in view of the large number of rickshaw pullers and the lack of experience in election procedures, it is stipulated that for every 100 rickshaw pullers, three impartial personnel will select one person as an elector. These electors (estimated to number about 400) will then elect two representatives to serve as directors of the Mutual Aid Society's board of directors. Detailed regulations for the selection of electors have also been stipulated. When electors nominate directors, they should personally go to the Mutual Aid Society's general office on East Jiaxing Road on the day of the election and follow the prescribed procedures. It is reported that the Public Works Department's board of directors has approved the rickshaw pullers' election method for the Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society.

Regarding the newly designed rickshaw style, rickshaw dealers and pullers have occasionally objected. After consideration by the Public Works Department's Special Committee on Rickshaws, according to the report of the Rickshaw Management Office, the recently finalized style has four improvements compared to the previous ones. Both rickshaw pullers and passengers have praised its convenience. The weight is lighter, the rider feels more comfortable, and the cost is not high, making it the most suitable vehicle on the market. Therefore, according to the office, the opposing voices from the outside have gradually decreased. The acting general manager of the Public Works Department also stated that the new-style rickshaw had previously been approved and implemented, and the number of rickshaws in circulation on the market is also increasing day by day. Therefore, today's re-raising of this issue is only to understand whether the issue should be reconsidered in light of external opposition and criticism. Subsequently, the Special Committee resolved that the issue should not be reconsidered, and this section has also been approved by the board of directors.

China Institute of Engineers: General Report on Association Affairs (III)

(XI) Regarding the matter of the National Construction Report, at last year's annual meeting, member Xu Yuanqi and others proposed that the general association should submit a National Construction Report at each annual meeting. At the 15th board meeting, Yin Enyong was designated to draft the method. The 16th board meeting resolved to pass the method, and after sending a letter to each branch to contribute their opinions, the National Construction Report will be edited and implemented starting in 1935. The method will also be published separately in the Engineering Weekly. (XII) Regarding the matter of industry books, member Zhao Fuling authored the book "Steel Reinforced Concrete," requesting that the association accept and publish it as a series. After inviting experts Li Keng and Li Xuehai to conduct a detailed review, the board of directors resolved to publish and distribute it. Additionally, member Lu Zengqi's book "Maintenance and Repair of Locomotive Boilers" was also approved by the board of directors after being reviewed by experts Chen Mingshou, Shi Jian, Wei Yifu, Cheng Xiaogang, Zhu Baofen, etc. (XIII) Regarding the addition of terms for machinery and electrical engineering, most of our country's engineering terms are translated from European and American countries. However, the translations are mixed and inconsistent, which greatly affects the development prospects of our country's engineering knowledge. In view of this, the association compiled and printed various engineering terms from 1928 to 1929, which scholars found convenient. The first edition of machinery and electrical engineering was a draft, and the number of copies was limited. However, due to the great need from all walks of life, a committee was specially organized, and members Gu Yuxiu, Liu Xianzhu, etc., were designated to revise the machinery terms, which had over 11,000 items, and the electrical terms, which had over 5,000 items, both of which were four or five times more than the first edition. Shortly after publication, they were sold out. At the invitation of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, the association selected review committee members.

Pengpu Defense Corps: The Truth About a Corps Member Shooting Another Corps Member; The Suspect, Zhu Shaofu, Claims the Deceased Had an Affair with His Wife; The Suspect, Bullets, etc., Were All Transferred to the Xinzha Public Security Bureau Yesterday

The case of Zhu Shaofu, a member of the Fourth Team, Zhangjiazhai Defense Post, Pengpu District Defense Corps in Zhabei, shooting his colleague, Wang Yutianxiang, was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, the confessions of the suspect Zhu Shaofu and Zhu's guarantor, Zou Guoguang, are recorded below. Zhu Shaofu confessed that he is 31 years old, from Siyang, and a member of the Pengpu Defense Corps. He has a wife, Liu, from Nanjing. In June of this year, she was seduced and taken away by Guoguang for more than ten days. Later, through mediation, Liu was returned. Unexpectedly, she fled again on August 23rd of the lunar calendar and disappeared without a trace. At that time, he still suspected that Zou had taken her away. On the 28th of last month, a friend surnamed Xu of Zou's came and told him that his wife was not taken by someone surnamed Zou, but was hidden by his colleague Yu Tianxiang. He asked him to discuss a solution at Zou's school. Later, when he went to Zou's school, Zou told him that Yu had a friend named Guan Shude. He could ask Guan to lure Yu out and kill him to avenge this. He immediately returned to the corps and explained the situation to Guan. At 11 p.m. on the 30th of last month, he called Guan to the corps and had Yu called out. He had been lying in ambush beforehand in the wilderness beside the Xiaochebang River near Zhangjiazhai, holding Guan's rifle, number 292. He shot and killed Yu. The bullet entered from the front chest and exited from the back. After Yu fell from the shot, he and Guan went forward to look at him. Guan then fired another shot at Yu and stabbed him three times with a sharp knife, one stab to the head and two stabs to the waist and back. Then Guan snatched the deceased's pistol and sent it to his guarantor, Zou Guoguang. Later, he thought that the revenge had been taken, so he returned to the post to sleep. Around 4 p.m. the next afternoon, members of the team came and arrested him at the tiger stove. Zou Guoguang confessed that he is 35 years old, from the same hometown as Zhu, and lives in the Public Works Bureau school on Sichuan Road as a "guan dou" (a type of police officer). At 12:40 a.m. on the 30th of September, Zhu Shaofu rang the doorbell. He initially suspected it was someone from Sandao Tou coming to sign a document, but when he opened the door, it was Zhu Shaofu. Zhu took out a pistol, number 21545, with three bullets, and put it there, saying Tian would take it. At that time, he saw blood on Zhu's undershirt and asked him where it came from. Zhu told him that Yu Tianxiang had just been killed. Upon hearing this, he immediately went to Zhangjiazhai with Zhu. He looked at the deceased's side and heard someone in the defense post say that the deceased had a pistol. Later, he returned to the school and sent the pistol to Yang Yucai. Detective Yang reported to the Deputy Captains Bao Ziying and Shi Zuhan, who dispatched the Deputy Squad Leaders Liu Changpei and Li Zhuqing, along with Yang Yucai, Sun Youzhi, Zang Ding, and Gao Changgui, and him to Zhangjiazhai, where they arrested Zhu Shaofu. They then dug up a rifle bullet and a sharp knife from the mud where the deceased had fallen and presented them as evidence. However, Guan Shude had already fled. After the team took the confession, yesterday they had already transported the suspect Zhu Shaofu, the reporter Zou Guoguang, along with a pistol, a sharp knife, three bullets, and one bullet head, to the Xinzha Sub-bureau. It was also heard that Zhu Shaofu said that his wife was taken away by Zou, which was a slander.

Yongtai Cigarette Factory Accused of Evading Taxes of Over 20,000 Gold Coins; 63 Account Books Were Not Stamped; The Factory Manager Failed to Appear in Court Yesterday After Being Summoned

The cigars sold by the Yongtai Cigarette Factory's distribution office at 326 Henan Road have not been taxed. After the General Inspectorate learned of this, it reported it to the First Special District Court. After dispatching detectives to the office for investigation the other day, it was discovered that from February of the 22nd year of the Republic [1933] to the end of last year, 6,289,681 cigars made by the factory had been sold, none of which had been taxed according to regulations. In addition, it was found that as many as 63 of the office's account books were not stamped, causing the state to lose 26,969.62 yuan in cigarette taxes, and the stamp tax also suffered considerable losses. Yesterday morning, the First Special Court summoned Zheng Qinyu, the factory manager from Zhongshan, Guangdong, for questioning, but Zheng refused to appear again and sent lawyer Yan Fangang to court to defend him. Public Security Bureau lawyer Jiang Baolian then presented the case, accusing the defendant of violating the Cigarette Tax Regulations and the Stamp Tax Regulations, and requested that he be punished according to law. Lawyer Yan then defended the defendant, saying that the cigars had been taxed by the factory when they were made. After the Yongtai Factory was destroyed in the "January 28th Incident," the cigars are now produced by the Senji Factory, which also pays taxes. Judge Zhan then postponed the hearing.

A Comprador of Tianli Foreign Firm Was Threatened by Bandits; A Bandit Arrived in a Car to Collect the Money; He Was Arrested by Detectives Who Were Waiting

Gong Ziqing, a comprador of Tianli Foreign Firm on Beijing Road, from Wuxi, lives at 78 Yayuan Road and runs the Ruidati Tiehang (iron shop) at 376 North Suzhou Road. Between the 25th and 28th of last month, he received two threatening letters from bandits, each containing a bullet, demanding 2,000 yuan. They also notified him by telephone to pay the money, otherwise they would take drastic measures. Gong reported the information to the police and negotiated on the phone. As a result, he agreed to pay 150 yuan, and arranged for someone to come to his house to collect it at 6 p.m. the day before yesterday. Zhou Yushan and Ye Yusi, the Chinese detective chiefs of the Jiashin Road Police Station in charge of the area, and Western detectives disguised themselves and waited near Zheng's house to observe the situation. Zhang Shengsan, a relative, waited with a check for 250 yuan. After a while, Zhang Yunlong, from Chongming, arrived in a Yunfei car number 12284. He got out of the car and calmly entered the house, presented a letter to Zhang Shengsan, obtained the check, and hurriedly left, giving a receipt. The Chinese and Western detectives rushed forward, arrested him, and took him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Bureau, detailed the case, saying that the defendant claimed at the police station that the principal offender was surnamed Shen, whom he met in a teahouse on Yuliao Bridge Road in Ximen. Later, he claimed that an old woman living in a thatched house on the same road had contacted him. His words were very hesitant. The threatening letters and receipts were not written by him. It was found that Gong Bingxian, who had previously been an accountant in the iron shop, had resigned for some reason and had been borrowing money from the owner from time to time. Recently, last month, he went to borrow money again but was refused and left in anger. It is possible that this person was responsible. It is recommended that the case be postponed for further investigation. Detective Zhou then reported the process of arresting the defendant and presented the letters and receipts. Gong Ziqing, the owner, was unable to attend due to illness, so his representative, Zhang Shengsan, testified about the situation at the time. Zhu Afu, the driver of the Yunfei car, said that he received a phone call at the branch on Ximen Road, asking him to send a car to the Red House Hospital on the same road. He drove the car to the entrance of the hospital and honked the horn twice. The defendant came from behind the car and said that he was going to Yayuan Road. He had an arrogant attitude. When the car arrived at the entrance of the owner's house, he jumped out and told him to wait a moment, and he went inside. After a while, he came out and was about to get into the car when he was arrested by the Chinese and Western detectives in the police station. The fare had not yet been paid. The defendant claimed that the letters were written by the principal offender, surnamed Shen, and the rest of his testimony was hesitant. Judge Xiao Xiefei ordered him to be detained and postponed the hearing for seven days for further verification.

Ding Ruichun Does Not Want Her Son to Be a Fatherless Child; Ten Years Ago, She Was a Prostitute and Had a Son with Chen Xianzhang; Now, as the Legal Guardian, She Sues to Confirm His Identity

The Tat Tiger Cart Industry Sends Another Letter to the Public Works Bureau, Requesting That They Order Their Subordinates Not to Detain Carts Without Reason

The Shanghai Tat Cart Industry Mutual Aid Association sent a letter to the Public Works Bureau yesterday, stating: "We respectfully inform you that members of our association have repeatedly reported that recently, various police stations have been detaining tat carts and tiger carts without reason, making it difficult for them to make a living and requesting protection. Our tat cart and tiger cart industry relies on human power to transport goods, working hard to maintain their meager livelihood. In this sluggish market, making a living and staying warm and fed is a constant concern. Those responsible for local security should be protecting their livelihoods. However, the various police stations do not understand this and often detain them without reason, which is inappropriate. We respectfully request that your bureau, as the highest administrative authority in the concession, is always concerned about the livelihoods of laborers. Therefore, we send this letter to request that you instruct your subordinates not to detain tat carts and tiger carts without reason. If a cart owner has done something wrong, please kindly guide them and do not cause them to be alarmed. This is our sincere prayer."

Creditors Lost Over 200,000 After Yongyuan Company Went Bankrupt; Tong Jitong Sues Shen Renqing for Joint Fraud for Defrauding Goods with Bad Checks

The general manager of Yongyuan Trading Company at 7 Yong'an Street, French Concession, was Jiang Tingfu from Ningbo. This year, he successively ordered a large batch of goods from major factories with postdated checks, which were transported to other ports for sale. On September 8, the company suddenly went bankrupt, and Jiang fled with the money without a trace. The total amount owed to the victims reached over 200,000 yuan. The creditors jointly organized a creditor group to recover the debt. At the same time, Tong Jitong, the manager of Zhufeng Company, filed a criminal self-accusation in the Second Special Court against Jiang Tingfu, the general manager of the company, and Shen Renqing, the manager from Hangzhou, for joint fraud, and filed an accompanying civil lawsuit. On the 18th of last month, the Municipal Public Security Bureau arrested Shen Renqing and transferred him to the local court for detention. Yesterday morning, the Second Special Court ordered the police to transfer Shen to the court for trial. The plaintiff, Tong Jitong, stated that Shen Renqing was introduced to purchase goods by a salesman, Gao Yangwu. After paying with a postdated check, he purchased a large amount of goods and then stopped shipping them. According to Shen, a telegram came from Guangdong, and he still needed to continue purchasing. On July 26, Gao suddenly disappeared for no reason. The company only owed more than 100 yuan, and only after pursuing the guarantor was it paid off. It was clear that the salesman colluded. On July 9, the company added goods and paid with a check for over 2,000 yuan, which was postponed repeatedly until the 4th. When a member of the company went to collect it when it was due, Shen suddenly said to come back in ten days. On the 8th, the company declared bankruptcy. The salary book showed that Jiang's salary was 181 yuan, Shen's was 151 yuan, and the rest of the staff only received 40 or 50 yuan. It was clear that Shen was the manager of the company, and there was documentary evidence to prove it. Shen Renqing stated that he was only a small employee of the company and had no involvement in the fraud. He had also been defrauded of a large sum of money and was also a creditor. He requested the court to arrest Jiang Tingfu. Judge Qiu verified the confession and ordered that the hearing be continued at 12 a.m. on the 12th and that the defendant be returned to custody. He also instructed Tong Jitong to present clear evidence that Shen was the manager. At this point, Judge Qiu re-examined Shen Renqing's self-accusation of Jiang Tingfu's fraud. Because Jiang had not been arrested, there was no way to try the case. He told Shen that the case could only be tried after the previous case was clarified or Jiang was arrested, and ordered the bailiffs to take Shen down and return him to custody.

Yao Amei's Corpse to Be Exhumed for Re-examination

Family Insists Boat Owner Beaten to Death; Boat Owner Suffers and Files Complaint with the Court

After Gong Haigen, a kiln cargo boat owner, had an argument with his hired boatman Yao Amei on the 19th of last month, Yao Amei fell into the river and died. The next day, the body was recovered, and the village head Zhao Ketang reported it to the local court for inspection. Prosecutor Xiao Jinying and others, commissioned by the court, arrived at the scene and determined that Yao Amei had indeed fallen into the river and died, filling out the form and ordering the coffin to be buried. It is now known that the family members of the deceased did not put the coffin lid on and repeatedly negotiated with the boat owner Gong Haigen, insisting that he had been beaten to death. Gong, unable to bear the burden, filed a complaint with the court requesting a thorough investigation. The wording of his complaint was roughly as follows: "Haigen owns a kiln cargo boat, which is docked in the Yangsi Port River. At 4:00 p.m. on September 19, the boatman Yao Amei suddenly lost his footing and drowned. His brother Yao Yinhai was on the boat (also a boatman) and immediately reported to the third squadron of the Yangsi Port Water Patrol, who ordered a quick rescue and reported all the people to the Public Security Bureau. Yao Yinhai confessed that his brother had indeed lost his footing and fallen into the water. According to witness Zhao Chengsheng, who testified that he witnessed the deceased losing his footing. Haigen was not at the scene when the accident occurred. After your court inspected the body, you ordered the coffin to be buried. Unexpectedly, many family members of the deceased came out, prevented the coffin from being covered, and destroyed the civilian's belongings. It was also heard that the family members of the deceased, in the quiet of the night, personally broke one of the deceased's feet and would try to deceive your court again, requesting another examination in order to blame the innocent. Left with no other choice, I file this complaint requesting a strict investigation." After the court received the complaint, yesterday morning it sent the police across the river to escort the coffin of Yao Amei, along with the family members of the deceased and the village head of the district, to the court. At 2:00 p.m., the coffin was transported by the Zhenru Forensic Institute's hearse to the Zhenru Institute, where it was opened for re-examination. If necessary, an autopsy will be performed.

At the Hongxia Fashion Company's fashion show held at the Grand Shanghai Ballroom, White House cigars were also given out, one for each person, filling the ballroom with fragrance.

Best-Selling Longevity Tonic Shou Er Kang. Since the German endocrine crystal Shou Er Kang tonic pills were promoted by the local Koten Foreign Firm, its ingredients are noble, and it has been recognized and proven effective by world-renowned doctors, resulting in a rapid increase in sales, almost at a rate of a thousand miles a day. All those who have taken it have praised it.

Popularity of Bubble Gum Commemorative Bags. Tian Tian Company, located at No. 36 Baker Road in this city, uses high-quality raw materials and scientific methods to produce bubble gum. It is sweet and delicious, quenches thirst, and generates saliva. The remaining gum can also be used to blow bubbles. It has been tested by the Hygiene Testing Institute to be completely free of harmful ingredients. This gum is most suitable for athletes. To arouse athletes' interest, the company has specially printed a small booklet of the National Games, containing valuable photos, the order of the Games, and past records. It is small and exquisite and easy to carry. It is packaged in a bag, each bag containing a dozen bubble gums, and sold for only ten cents each. It is sold at the Sincere Company United Promotion Market, the Yong'an Company Rooftop Garden, and various designated middle schools. During the Games, it will also be sold at booth No. 19 in the stadium. Currently, there are many buyers at various sales outlets, all eager to get a first look.

Publishing World

History of Economic Thought. Deng Yisheng, who holds a master's degree in economics from London, England, has been teaching economics at various universities in Shanghai for many years. He has now compiled his usual lectures into a book entitled "History of Economic Thought," which was published at the end of last month and is sold by the World and Great East Bookstores. Priced at one yuan, the book contains eight chapters, starting from mercantilism and ending with John Stuart Mill, which is suitable for a one-semester university course. The method of compilation is excellent, the analysis of theories is thorough, and the ideas are sharp, new, and critically correct. It is truly a unique work in Chinese economic books.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong and Guozhou would be sunny to cloudy, with strong northwesterly to northerly breezes. The Yangtze River basin would be cloudy, with morning fog and northwesterly to northeasterly winds. The East China Sea would have southeasterly winds. Korea would have cyclones and rain due to a low pressure system moving northeast. The highest temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 81.1 degrees, and the lowest was 67.5 degrees. The highest temperature on the same day last year was 70.7 degrees, and the lowest was 63.9 degrees.

Venue Division Regulations for the National Games - Player Practice Rules for Each Venue

Available for practice from the 5th to the 8th. Registration with the Venue Division is required to arrange order.

With the National Games opening soon, athletes from all over are arriving in Shanghai one after another. The Venue and Equipment Division of the Games Committee has specially stipulated the opening hours of each sports venue for athletes to practice. The details are as follows: (1) Track and Field - from October 5th to 8th, from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM daily. (2) Swimming Pool - from October 5th to 8th, from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM daily. (3) Gymnasium Basketball Court - from October 5th to 9th, from 7:40 AM to 5:40 PM daily. Each team's practice time is 40 minutes. (Each team must first register with the Venue Division (to arrange the practice order)). (4) Baseball and Softball Fields - from October 7th to 9th, from 3:00 PM daily. (5) Soccer Field - from October 5th to 8th, from 4:00 PM daily. (6) Tennis and Volleyball Courts - from October 5th to 8th, from 7:30 AM to 5:30 PM daily.

Gymnasium Practice Rules

(1) Male and female basketball teams from each unit who wish to practice basketball in the gymnasium must first register with the Venue Division. (2) Practice dates are from the morning of the 5th of this month to the evening of the 9th. (3) Within the above dates, the number of practice sessions per unit is limited to two. (4) Each practice time is 40 minutes. (5) When practicing, each unit should abide by the scheduled time and not extend it.

Tennis and Volleyball Practice Rules

(1) Male and female tennis and volleyball teams from each unit who wish to practice should first register with the Venue Equipment Division to arrange the practice order to avoid confusion. (2) Practice dates are from October 5th to 8th, from 7:30 AM to 12:00 PM and from 1:00 PM to 5:30 PM daily. (3) Within the stipulated practice dates and times above, each volleyball team can practice four times, and each tennis team can practice up to three times. (5) Each practice time is set at one and a half hours. (6) When practicing, each unit and team should abide by the scheduled time and not extend it to avoid interfering with the practice time of the next unit.

Transportation Arrangements for the National Games

Traffic routes for all types of vehicles have been stipulated. Prices and times for special trains on both routes have also been set.

During the National Games, traffic to and from the venues will inevitably be congested. The Games Committee has specially formulated transportation arrangements. Traffic routes for all types of vehicles have been stipulated to avoid confusion. The details of these transportation arrangements are recorded below:

(1) Private Cars

(A) From Zhabei and the Concessions to the Venue - (1) Vehicles from the eastern district should enter Jungong Road via Yangshupu, pass Wuquan Road, the front of the Municipal Government, and Sanmin Road to the northern parking lot of the stadium. (2) Vehicles from the Hongkou district should take North Sichuan Road to Jiangwan Road, West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, and Songhu Road to the northern parking lot of the stadium. Alternatively, vehicles can take North Henan Road to Baoshan Road, Jiangwan Road, West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, and Songhu Road to the northern parking lot of the stadium. (3) Vehicles from the western district should take Zhongyou Road and West Baoxing Road to Shuidian Road, Xiangyin Road, and Songhu Road to the northern parking lot of the stadium.

(B) From the Venue to Zhabei and the Concessions - (1) From the northern parking lot of the stadium, take Funan Right Road, Xiangyin Road, and head east into Jungong Road, or head west through Huangxing Road into Ningguo Road. After 8:00 PM, vehicles can take Xiangyin Road west and enter Diswei Road via Qimei Road. (2) From the northern parking lot of the stadium, pass the front of the Municipal Government, Wuquan Road, and enter Jungong Road to Yangshupu.

(2) Taxis

(A) From Zhabei and the Concessions to the Venue - (1) Vehicles from the Hongkou district should take North Henan Road, Baoshan Road, Jiangwan Road, West Qingti Association Road, Xiangyin Road, and Songhu Road to the Zhengyi Road parking lot. Alternatively, vehicles can take North Sichuan Road, Jiangwan Road, West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, and Songhu Road to the Zhengyi Road parking lot. (2) Vehicles from Jungong Road will follow the same route as private cars. (3) Vehicles from Zhongshan Road will follow the same route as private cars.

(B) From the Zhengyi Road Parking Lot to Zhabei or the Concessions - From the Zhengyi Road parking lot, take Guowei Road, Xiangyin Road, Qimei Road, and Diswei Road.

(C) The fare is $1.20 each time, and tips are at the customer's discretion. The usual tip is 20 cents.

(3) Public Buses

During the Games, Zhabei Huashang Public Bus Company will continue to operate the original Routes 1, 4, and 5 and will add additional special buses to reach the Zhengtong Road parking lot directly.

(A) The bus stops for Routes 1, 4, and 5 are at the intersection of Qiujiang Road and Baoshan Road. The buses will depart every 37 minutes starting at 6:00 AM each morning, with a total of 14 round trips for each route daily. The fare is 41 copper coins each time.

(B) The special bus stop is also at the intersection of Qiujiang Road and Baoshan Road. Buses will depart as soon as they are full. The fare is 20 cents per person each time.

(C) Routes - (1) To the venue, take Qiujiang Road and Baoshan Road, pass West Baoxing Road, Shuidian Road, Xiangyin Road, and Songhu Road to the Zhengtong Road parking lot. (2) Returning, from the Zhengtong Road parking lot, take Guowei Road south, Xiangyin Road west, enter East Sports Association Road, Baoshan Road, and Baochang Road to the intersection of Qiujiang Road and Baoshan Road.

(4) Converted Passenger Trucks

(A) To the venue, take West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, and Bicheng Road to the Zhengtong Road parking lot.

(B) Returning, from the Zhengtong Road parking lot, take Guowei Road, Xiangyin Road, East Sports Association Road, and Tongli Road to West Sports Association Road.

(5) Rickshaws, Handcarts, Small Carts, and "Tiger" Carts

The above four types of vehicles are not allowed to pass during the following times and on the following routes: (A) 9:00 AM to 2:00 PM and 5:00 PM to 8:00 PM on the Double Tenth Day; and 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM and 5:00 PM to 8:00 PM daily during the rest of the Games. (B) Baoshan Road, West Sports Association Road, Qimei Road, and the entire city center area.

(6) Bicycles

Only the following routes are allowed: (A) Zhongshan Road, West Baoxing Road, Jiangwan Racecourse, Ye Family Garden, heading east on Songshi Road to Sanmin Road, parking in the bicycle lot. (B) Jungong Road, Wuquan Road, in front of the Municipal Government, Sanmin Road, to the bicycle lot. (C) Ningwu Road, Yinxiang Port, Ma Baoshan Road, Xiangyin Road, heading west, Funan Left Road, in front of the Municipal Government, Sanmin Road, to the bicycle lot.

(7) Prices for Temporary Third-Class Passenger Trains Between Various Stations on Both Routes and Sanmin Road Station

Price List for Temporary Third-Class Passenger Tickets Between Various Stations on Both Routes and Sanmin Road Station

(8) Fares for Each Station on the Songhu Branch Line

With the approval of the Municipal Government, the two railway bureaus have extended the Songhu Road branch line to reach the National Games venue. Once the platform and ticket office construction at each station is completed, it will be officially opened. The fares from each station to the stadium are set as follows: (1) One-Way: Shangbei, 15 cents; Tiantong'an, 10 cents; Jiangwan, 5 cents; Wusong Town, 20 cents; Paotaiwan, 25 cents. Various School Students and Staff to Visit the National Games: Regulations

Tickets Priced at One-Quarter, Classes Suspended for One to Two Days

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has issued a public notice regarding the arrangements for group ticket purchases at reduced prices for students and staff of universities, middle schools, and primary schools in the city to attend the National Games, as well as the allocation methods and revisions to the suspension of classes period. The notice states that the 6th National Games have been scheduled to open on National Day, and the Bureau has established and announced attendance regulations to facilitate group visits by teachers, students, and staff of all levels of schools in the city. The price of admission tickets has been negotiated with the National Games organizing committee to be reduced to one-quarter of the original price, i.e., one-quarter of the ordinary ticket price, but only for attendance at the athletics field. The ordinary admission ticket prices are divided into four levels: one yuan, six jiao, four jiao, and two jiao. However, there are not many one-yuan tickets. The Bureau has allocated them appropriately, with one-yuan tickets primarily for universities, six-jiao tickets primarily for middle schools, and four-jiao and two-jiao tickets primarily for primary schools. All students attending must wear the prescribed uniforms on the date of attendance and enter the venue with their leaders holding the Bureau's registration certificate, after purchasing reduced-price tickets at the purchasing point, and each person will be given one ticket. At the same time, they will enter the venue. Furthermore, according to Item 2 of the Bureau's regulations on school staff and students' attendance, students of all levels of schools may suspend classes for half a day on the date of their scheduled visit to the National Games. Now, because the competition programs may be held all day, and the number of attendees from each school may be too large, with one visit being insufficient for distribution, the suspension of classes should be changed to one to two days to facilitate attendance. This notice is hereby issued for public knowledge.

Swimming Competition: Hong Kong-Shanghai Chinese Alliance Defeats Western Alliance by a Large Margin

Western Alliance Manpower Scattered and Loses Badly 9-18. 200-Meter Relay Breaks National Record.

The swimming competition between the Hong Kong-Shanghai Chinese Alliance and the Shanghai Western Alliance was held again last night at the city swimming pool. The Chinese Alliance defeated the Western Alliance by a large margin with a score of 18-9. The score difference was exactly one-fold. The Western Alliance easily lost because of its incomplete manpower and the fact that all of its members were second-rate athletes. The women's group lacked Western women entirely, so Yang Xiuqiong and others had to perform alone. The water polo match, where interest was concentrated, was won by the Chinese Alliance by a score of 4-1. Jening and Brunnet's comical diving performance was humorous and elicited applause and laughter from the two thousand spectators, making it an interesting highlight of the competition. The number of spectators last night exceeded that of the previous night.

Fifty Meters Lost Unfortunately

The 50-meter freestyle was one of the most exciting scenes in the competition. Western Alliance's Britten was a Shanghai Interport athlete this year and was narrowly defeated by Chen Zhenxing in Hong Kong. He was quite unwilling to accept this. The two met again last night and competed with all their might. Unfortunately, Zhenxing was a little late falling into the water, and the distance was too short. Britten defeated him by a shoulder's length at the finish line, which was a pity.

100 Meters Breaks Record

Chen Zhenxing, who finished second in the 50-meter event, showed his skills in the 100-meter freestyle. Western Alliance's Stankowski was able to resist stubbornly. At 80 meters, he was neck and neck with Chen Zhenxing, indistinguishable. It was not until the last 15 meters that Chen jumped ahead, finally defeating Stankowski by a distance of three meters. Li Luomin was third, and Liang Xingsheng was absent. According to the record, Chen's time was 1 minute 6.7 seconds, only one-tenth of a second behind the national record of 1 minute 6.6 seconds.

Chinese Alliance Sweeps Backstroke and Breaststroke

The Chinese Alliance swept the 100-meter backstroke and 100-meter breaststroke. Only one Westerner, Ryan, participated in the breaststroke, and one, Belins, participated in the backstroke. As a result, both of them were completely defeated, being third-rate athletes in the Western Alliance.

Women's Competition Changed to Performance

The women's competition was temporarily changed to a performance competition due to the absence of Western women. Yang Xiuqiong, Yang Xiuzhen, and Chen Fengying first performed the 50-meter freestyle, with Xiuqiong first, Xiuzhen second, and Chen third. The time was 36.7 seconds, better than Yang's national record of 38.2 seconds, but not as good as the 36-second record from the previous night. Next, Yang Xiuqiong performed the 100-meter backstroke alone, without timing. Qu Enzhao also performed the 200-meter breaststroke alone. Because there was no competition, the time was 3 minutes 49 seconds. Qu is only 13 years old and broke the national record for the 200-meter breaststroke in Hong Kong with a time of 3 minutes 35 seconds. Qu is one of the promising talents in the National Games.

Diving Performance is Comical and Humorous

The diving performance first featured artistic diving, with participants Henbo, Glick, Belins, Huang Xiying, and Zha Zhurui. The Westerners are all experts in this field, not only are their poses beautiful, but also their patterns are varied. Huang Xihan is also comparable, but slightly inferior. Next, Jening and Brunnet performed comical diving, dressed as clowns, performing various comical falls into the water on the diving board, eliciting laughter and applause from the audience. The two are not only humorous, but also have good diving skills.

Relay Lost But Results are Remarkable

The lineup of the 200-meter relay was as follows: (1) Xu Heng, (2) Zeng Hefu, (3) Li Luomin, (4) Chen Zhenxing. The first two were neck and neck with the Westerners. Unfortunately, Li Luomin was a little late falling into the water, so the fourth person, Chen Zhenxing, could not catch up. They lost to Britten by five meters. The Chinese Alliance's time was 1 minute 58.6 seconds, which, although second, broke the national record of 2 minutes 1.1 seconds. The Western Alliance's time was 1 minute 57.6 seconds, a difference of one second.

Water Polo Match Won by Chinese Alliance

In the final water polo match, the Chinese Alliance won 4-2. Their coordination was extremely skilled, and their shooting was also good. It is said that the Western Alliance's participants were the B team of the Asian Youth Water Polo team, with no coordination at all. Their strength was too far apart from that of the Chinese Alliance. In the first half, the Chinese Alliance quickly scored three goals. In the second half, the Western Alliance scored one goal, and the Chinese Alliance also scored. The Western Alliance scored another goal, resulting in a score of 4-2. The Chinese Alliance lineup was as follows:

Zhou Dayun

Chen Ziqing Zhang Yunguang Zeng Hefu

Zhou Ruiqin Li Luomin Xu Heng

Jiangxi Province Athlete Lineup

Men's and Women's High Jump Results are Very Outstanding. Swimming Team Goes to Jiangsu and Zhejiang for Friendly Matches.

Nanchang Correspondence - Jiangxi's participation in previous National Games has resulted in very few points, and even zero points in some cases. In recent years, the authorities have paid considerable attention to sports and are rapidly catching up. In particular, President Chiang's stationing in Jiangxi to suppress bandits has made sports one of the key elements of national revival, promoting and urging it without reservation. Sports fields have been added in various counties and cities throughout the province, and swimming, archery, and equestrianism have emerged in response to the trend, becoming popular everywhere. Sports are no longer limited to students, and soldiers, civil servants, and citizens also participate. The selection of representatives for this year's Games, which leans towards bank and agency staff, soldiers, and freelancers, is a clear indication of this.

Jiangxi's participation in the 6th National Games began on September 11th, with competitions and selections organized by county and city. All athletes were then trained and tested. All staff members were also appointed by the Department of Education.

Staff

Provincial Representative (Department of Education, He Jianqian, General Leader, Public Stadium Director) Yu Yongzuo, Deputy Leaders Xing Lufel, Deng Beishun, General Managers Gong Zhenfan, Shen Rongzhao, Shi Meikui, Men's Track and Field and All-Around Coach Yin Xianmin, Manager Tao Youmei, Basketball Coach Wu Yunlong, Manager Lin Xingfang, Volleyball Coach Chuan Bingyue, Manager Chen Ying, Tennis Coach Chen Shimian, Soccer Coach Yang Demi, Manager Wang Youmin, Traditional Chinese Martial Arts Liang Yaoting, Seawater Swimming Coach Lu Gaohui, Women's Track and Field Coach Li Zonghao, Manager Lu Xunxue, Women's Basketball Coach Wu Qiu, Manager Tao Lihua.

Track and Field

Because of the selection of the elite from the Air Force, various military units, and bank agencies, the strength of the athletes is better than in previous Games. This time, they may be able to wash away the shame of zero points. The lineups are as follows: 100 meters, Liu Jiayu, 11.8 seconds; 400 meters, Xu Jiyun, 57 seconds; 400-meter hurdles, 1 minute 5.7 seconds; middle hurdles, Jin Huaizhi, 1 minute 4.3 seconds; high jump, Yang Baoluo, 1.83 meters, Zhou Shijian, 1.82 meters; pole vault, Leng Peiji, 3.15 meters; discus, Leng Peiji, 32 meters; javelin, Yang Baoluo, 41.72 meters; triple jump, Huang Bogang, 12.30 meters. On the women's side, the Provincial First Women's Vocational School almost swept the field, with outstanding athletes such as Hu Meixiu's discus at 23.06 meters, Liao Fang's high jump at 1.29 meters, and Cheng Maolan's 16-pound shot put at 8.76 meters. Many of the others broke provincial and Central China records.

Swimming

The province's strength is quite good. The athletes are mostly veterans from the Bolang Team, Lizhi Branch, and New Life Club swimming teams, with well-trained skills. In the recent disaster relief competitions held in Jiangxi with Hunan and Hubei, the top three places were swept by the province. They have now departed for Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui to participate in friendly matches, with all proceeds from ticket sales going to disaster relief. Their results are as follows: Bu Liang's 50-meter freestyle, 35 seconds; 100-meter freestyle, 1 minute 26 seconds; Liu Lingci's 100-meter backstroke, 1 minute 42 seconds; Chao Zhikui's 200-foot breaststroke, 3 minutes; Wan Ronggui's 400 meters, 7 minutes 20 seconds; 1500 meters, 29 minutes 52 seconds. Other events such as bound hands and feet swimming, escaping from burlap sacks, and artistic diving also have good results. This time, they will definitely show their skills.

Ball Games

A mixed system is adopted, no longer with representatives from a certain city or county attending. The men's tennis players are Li Yunyan, Wang Yinghuai, Zhu Qinghe, and Mao Linkui. The men's basketball team includes Li Yuelong, Zhang Shao, Meng Yukun, Shen Huanqing, Meng Guangxin, Liu Zongwu, Shi Fen, Fan Zhisui, Li Xihu, and Zhang Xianqiu. The men's volleyball team consists of twelve athletes including Xu Jiepei. The above are mostly elites from various military units, schools, the Aviation Commission Air Force, and amateur athletes. The women's ball games are based on Nanchang Women's Middle School and Women's Vocational Baoling, with outstanding participants from various counties only participating in basketball. The rest were not sent due to a lack of talent. Therefore, this time, they uphold the principle of selecting the best, not the most.

Education News

Hubei Department of Education Establishes Health Education Division

(Hankou, 1st) - In order to promote the implementation of health education in schools throughout the province, the Hubei Department of Education has specially established a Health Education Division, with Xu Shouchu as the director, which was officially established on October 1st.

Shanghai Municipal Council Education Department Pays Attention to the Future of Students

The Shanghai Municipal Council Education Department recently held a meeting to discuss two important matters: one was the eyesight of students. The head of the Municipal Council Health Department had submitted a detailed report on the poor eyesight of students in the various Chinese schools established by the Municipal Council, arguing that the parents of the students should be vigorously educated to promote their awareness. The trachoma treatment that has been effective is also accompanied by the treatment of other eye diseases. In the future, full attention should be paid to the treatment of trachoma first, and ordinary eyesight treatment will be considered at a later date. According to the report of the school medical director of the Municipal Council, Chinese students' parents have a deep prejudice against children wearing glasses. The remedy is to issue notices and persuasion, but there is no good method. Students from poor families often cannot afford to buy glasses, and ordinary families still consider glasses a luxury item and not a necessity for children. Therefore, the Education Department's discussion of the eyesight problem of students argued that it should continue to work with the Health Department. Furthermore, the Education Department also discussed the outlets for out-of-school children and the supervision of students after school. The Education Department had previously commissioned Mr. Harris to investigate the facilities in London, England, for this matter. Mr. Harris's report has been submitted to the Education Department. During the last meeting, it was said that only the outlet of students could be tried in Shanghai, but the scope was too broad, and it was doubtful whether the Education Department's strength could be competent and happy. However, it seemed that the Chinese education authorities were working hard, and the development of vocational education and the introduction of institutional services were both major initiatives. If the Shanghai Municipal Council in the Public Concession could urge the existing institutions in the Concession to carry out these initiatives, it could achieve twice the result with half the effort. It was then resolved that the Education Department Director should prepare a report on the vocational guidance facilities in the Chinese and Western schools and discuss it in the long run. The above record of the Education Department meeting has been read by the Board of Directors yesterday.

Municipal Bureau of Education Solicits Privately Written Children's Books

To Participate in the National Children's Goods Exhibition

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a public notice stating that it had received a letter from the National Children's Year Implementation Committee (Order No. 176), which stated that the committee, in accordance with the provisions of the General Outline of the Children's Year Implementation Measures, would hold a National Children's Books Exhibition in December of this year. Among the committee's measures regarding the collection of exhibits, there was a category of privately written children's books. The collection of these books was decided by the committee's fifth congress as follows: (1) Request the local Children's Year Implementation Committees and provincial and municipal education departments to collect on its behalf. (2) Advertise in newspapers to solicit from private individuals, recorded on file. A corresponding record letter is hereby sent for your reference and processing, and please send the books collected on its behalf to the committee before November for display and exhibition. In addition to informing all subordinate schools and institutions to widely solicit, this public notice is hereby issued to inform all. All privately written children's books must be submitted to the Bureau before the end of October for verification and approval.

Meeting of the Secondary School Association

The Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Association held its 51st general meeting on the 28th of this month at noon at the Gongdelin Restaurant. The principals of the following schools attended: Provincial Shanghai High School, Lida Academy, Qingxin Middle School, Yucai, Jingye, Huahua, Patriotic Girls' Middle School, Minli Middle School, Nanyang Middle School, Qingxin Girls' Middle School, Dazhong, Guangxia, Wusong Junior High School, Kaiming, Qiaoguang, Wuben Girls' Middle School, Chengzhong, Guanghua High School, Fudan Experimental High School, Fudan High School, Hujiang High School, Xinmin, Chinese Vocational, McLaren, etc. Zheng Xigu chaired the meeting, and Cheng Kuanzheng recorded it. First, the chairman reported on (1) the association's founding purpose, (2) the association's progress, and (3) the association's financial receipts and expenditures. Next, the following were discussed: (1) a motion to amend the charter, which was passed; (2) a motion to re-elect the standing committee, which was resolved through a vote to elect the Provincial Shanghai High School, Guanghua High School, Chinese Vocational, Fudan High School, and McLaren Middle School as standing committee members, and Hujiang High School, Wuben Girls' Middle School, and Jingye Middle School as alternate members; (3) a motion to formulate a general outline of the work plan for this academic year, which was resolved as follows: I. For students: (1) hold a current affairs essay competition, (2) implement military management, and (3) promote the balanced development of mind and body to correct the past habit of overemphasizing intellectual training. A declaration will be issued in the name of the Association, and it will be submitted to the Ministry of Education. The above three items will be carried out by the standing committee. II. For faculty and staff: (1) hold academic lectures, to be organized by the standing committee; (2) organize a Northwest Education Tour Group, open to voluntary participation; (3) promote mutual visits among schools; (4) continue to study history and geography teaching materials; (5) formulate key points for spiritual talks, solicit opinions from various schools, and be drafted by the standing committee; (6) promote teachers' wearing of uniforms. III. Other aspects: (1) promote the use of domestic goods; (2) discuss common problems among schools; (3) appoint members to review the association's income and expenditure plan for the 23rd year. The meeting adjourned at 4 PM, and it was decided to appoint Jingye and Kaiming schools.

Little Boy (64)

— Original by Ms. Alcott of America, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

At that time, Frank was still studying. When he finished leaving the study room, he smelled smoke. He rushed upstairs and saw this scene, rising like a cloud from the left wing of the house. He felt there was no time to wake others, so he immediately ran into the room and dragged the two children out of the blazing bed, pouring all the water he could find onto the flames. The fire subsided slightly, but it didn't go out completely. The two children, dragged to the cold hallway, had already regained consciousness and began to scream frantically. Mrs. Pei arrived on the scene immediately. Soon, Mr. Lai rushed out of his room, shouting "Fire!" His voice startled the entire house. A group of little white-clad spirits, looking frightened, gathered in the doorway. For a moment, everyone seemed to be overwhelmed by fear, not knowing what to do.

Soon, Mrs. Pei was the first to regain her alertness. She ordered Nasui to take care of the burned children, and told Frank and Mr. Lai to bring several buckets of wet clothes from downstairs. She immediately threw these wet clothes onto the bed, carpet, and curtains, because these were now burning fiercely and about to spread to all four walls.

Most of the children just stood there watching, only Tang En and Ai Mi bravely rushed to the bathroom to get water, and helped pull down the dangerous curtains.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

The National Products Industry Should Take a Long-Term View

— Yang An

Today, the national products industry should rely on its own efforts to open up new avenues and compete with global industry and commerce, so as not to be subject to natural elimination. It must not be confined to the mainland, engaging solely in imitation, echoing others, and thus falling into a dead end. For example, regarding the matter of exhibitions, the reporter has repeatedly offered earnest advice, suggesting that organizers should change course as early as possible and explore new paths. However, the general public is blinded by small profits and driven by a desire to win, holding one exhibition after another, continuously. Disregarding the opposition of local merchants and the rejection of local groups, they are seen as bandits, only creating resentment among local merchants who are enthusiastic about selling national products. They brazenly ignore this, what kind of plan is this that things would get to this point? I have often said that if national product exhibitions are not improved, the national products exhibited in the future will become annoying to various places, and merchants in various places may be unwilling to sell national products. The organizers of these events, using various factories to increase their own importance, rely on the reputation of tax exemption to engage in sales, without considering that local vendors are not unpatriotic, they already have the same products, and usually sell them to local users. Now the organizers, disregarding the meaning of the name, use the name of exhibitions to carry out dumping. Selling the same products at different prices, they may benefit themselves, but what about the local merchants? Therefore, I have often advised national product merchants that instead of joining exhibitions and creating resentment among merchants in various places, it is better to send staff to various places to investigate and liaise, listen to the opinions of merchants and the psychology of customers in various places, in order to gain general goodwill and criticism, so as to improve their own products. Being fond of pursuing and joining the fun, only to lose customers in various places, is not only useless, but also harmful. I sincerely advise you, please forgive my bluntness. Furthermore, today the national products industry should take a long-term view and pay attention to international trade. To curb import surplus, we must first encourage exports. The Nanyang area is a huge outlet for our country's national products industry. Currently, the Ministry of Industry and the International Trade Bureau, and the China Industrial Foreign Trade Association are working hard to support national product manufacturers and promote national products. Recently, Mr. Zhang Yujiu, the new secretary-general of the International Trade Association, is the most enthusiastic comrade for national products. The reporter knows that he is very willing to serve the national products industry. Our national products industry should cooperate with him earnestly. When there are various issues, we can discuss them with him and surely achieve satisfactory results.

Heartfelt Words from Leading Figures in the National Products Industry

— Kang Jianzhai's Wife

The other day, I happened to see in the Xin Ye Bao a conversation in which Huang Jiping interviewed several leading figures in the Shanghai industrial sector. These leading figures, who are working hard to promote national products, seem to be front-line generals who are firmly entrenched in our country's external economic front, fighting to the death. The words they spoke were bitter and piercing to the heart. Here, I will repeat their words, despite being accused of rehashing old news, and reveal them to everyone as a wake-up call.

"...Speaking of woollen cloth, our country is really losing a lot. Many young people who wear suits, especially college students, despise domestic woollen cloth. They insist on wearing foreign goods. Alas! What Student National Products Year, the future is really unimaginable." - (Words of Mr. Liu Hongsheng)

"...If you close your eyes and smoke various Chinese and foreign cigarettes, you can't tell which is superior or inferior. The taste is not much different either. So I think people who like to smoke foreign cigarettes have no other purpose than to show off their wealth." - (Words of Mr. Wu Yun Chu)

"The Mainland Department Store and China National Products Company have everything, but they don't go in, they want to drill into the three major companies to buy foreign goods. What can you do? Try visiting government agencies and noble families, and the cigarettes and alcohol they have are often foreign goods. It seems that only in this way can they show off their wealth..." - (Words of Mr. Fang Yexian)

"...The sales of light bulbs are worse year by year. The main reason is that the market is shrinking. Like the loss of the Northeast, national products have disappeared. The current North China is like the Northeast; in short, once the situation changes, national products will lose their livelihood..." - (Words of Mr. Hu Xiyuan)

"...Promoting national products has been effective among people in the lower and middle classes. Only the upper class, they have the money, as long as they eat comfortably, they don't care whether it's foreign or domestic. Such inferior mentality is seen in the upper class, which is really disheartening..." - (Words of Mr. Wang Xingyao)

"Japanese people are ashamed of smoking foreign cigarettes and using foreign goods; Chinese people are proud of smoking foreign cigarettes and using foreign goods..." - (Words of Mr. Pan Yangyao)

Currently, tensions are running high between Europe and Africa, and war is imminent. According to the declaration of the Shanghai Banking Research Department, after the outbreak of war, our country's native products transported to European countries and North Africa, such as peanuts, tea, beans, eggs, silk, carpets, and straw mats, will have their sales greatly reduced due to the obstruction of transportation in the Mediterranean Sea. If the war lasts for a year, the export value will decrease by more than 70 million yuan. As for the impact of the war on the situation in East Asia, that is another matter.

We are so far behind in the military preparations for modern warfare that we cannot defend ourselves. The economic war, which is increasingly encroaching, has long been mired in chaos. If we don't try our best to use national products for the necessities of daily life, then we are steadily heading towards the path of destruction!

I know that most newspaper readers, in addition to looking at the dynamics of the international and domestic situation, all kinds of surprising social news, entertaining short articles, movie magazines, and picture magazines, rarely pay attention to propaganda articles that are didactic and not sensational. Especially the so-called rich and noble upper class, and the trendy young people, they themselves do not care, and the words of others' advice cannot enter their ears. Then what else is there to say!

The Past and Future of Student National Products Year

— Zhu Weixuan

Oh, how grand and prosperous was the Student National Products Year! In the blink of an eye, two-thirds of it has passed, but when we look back at the achievements of the past, it is really somewhat disheartening. Students, not only have they not achieved significant results or made substantial contributions in this Student National Products Year, but also contradictory, lazy, and distorted situations are constantly unfolding before us. This is truly not only a stain on the Student National Products Year, but also a great shame for the entire Chinese nation!

As for the most contradictory point of the Student National Products Year, nothing is more contradictory than the Western suits and leather shoes of college students, entering and leaving dance halls, opening champagne, eating Western food, chewing Wrigley's gum, and applying Stetson hair cream, none of which are not completely authentic imported goods. Although in a certain period in the past, some people advocated banning college students from dancing, but times have changed, and now college students are once again active in dance halls!

Middle school students have always been very diligent and willing to work hard in social group activities; but in this Student National Products Year, there seems to be no special achievements either. Perhaps because college students are going against the grain, completely forgetting the important mission of the Student National Products Year? So they also follow suit, abandoning their responsibilities. For the national products movement, not only have they not actively developed and promoted it externally; but most of their own desks are still filled with Waterman's ink, and they have Parker fountain pens inserted in their chests, completely placing the arduous responsibility of the Student National Products Year behind their minds!

As for elementary school students, if their parents and teachers do not constantly instill national products education in them, then they probably don't understand the meaning of the so-called Student National Products Year at all. We can often see kindergarten students excitedly playing with foreign toys. This cannot help but make me sigh three times and put down my pen!

The past is gone, the future can be pursued. The constant appearance of these many distorted events in the past certainly makes us feel heartbroken and sigh; but this is definitely not the passive sigh that can help matters. We want to hope for the future; in the next three or four months, we want to redeem our past numb and indifferent sins with real and powerful achievements!

Students across the country! The future masters of the country, you are educated intellectuals, you should stand on the position of the foreknowers and the foresighted. From now on, not only should you set an example by using national products everywhere; but also persuade your family members and even anyone in society to recognize and use national products. At the same time, you should constantly and always instill national products education and common sense in elementary school students, so that the impression of national products will be deeply imprinted in their young minds, and they will develop the habit of using national products from an early age!

Finally, there is one more point that is worth bringing up for discussion: that is, the yearbooks and graduation albums published by major middle schools every year are mostly gold-plated on the cover and beautifully bound. When examining the paper, it all comes from foreign countries. Not only is the profit outflowing every year, which is considerable, but also in the current Student National Products Year, it is extremely contradictory that the booklets, which include the essence of the entire school, are printed on non-national products paper. Once it is passed into the hands of foreigners, it will be ridiculed even more! Therefore, I also hope that those in charge will consider and pay attention to this point before printing, and do not just pursue the beauty of the form and appearance, but disregard the value of the publication itself, leaving a great stain!

We Need National Product Pen Nibs

— Ji Yu

To study science, we cannot only rely on a writing brush. Precisely for this reason, pen nibs have formed a very good market for us. We cannot watch box after box of pen nibs coming in and batches of silver going out, so we must shout, "We need national product pen nibs"!

Those who hear it may say: "You know how to use foreign pen nibs, aren't the Chinese fountain pens very good? Look! This is Huafu, this is Xinmin, this is Doctor..." But this friend's words are too "freehand". Fountain pens, even if they are Chinese fountain pens, how much does a pen cost? In this time when five hundred mu of money can only afford one person to study, who has extra money to buy fountain pens? We cannot afford fountain pens, but we need pen nibs.

Here, let me offer some suggestions so that we have good national product pen nibs to use.

(1) The government or merchants should set up factories to manufacture them. For now, let's start with middle school students and go up to college students, not counting others. We know that there are currently 553,414 middle and college students in China. If each person uses one per month, one dozen per year, then the sales of pen nibs will be these 500,000+ dozens. In this large number, if the government or merchants are willing to set up a factory to manufacture them, then even if they adhere to the principle of small profits, I think the benefits will certainly be many. Moreover, the people who use pen nibs are not only students, and in addition to pen nibs, the factory can also produce things such as pen holders, etc.

(2) Fountain pen factories can also produce pen nibs, which is also a very good method, because the nib of a fountain pen and the nib of an ordinary pen are not much different in form. If fountain pen factories are willing to use a part of the mechanical force, and slightly modify the machines to manufacture ordinary pen nibs, then the capital used to modify the machines, which is very little money, can definitely get many rewards.

I hope that the above methods, (1) or (2), can be realized in the shortest possible time. Pen nibs are small, but we must not ignore them. We must know that their leakage is very large.

Reminiscences of Moon Viewing at Nanhu Lake and Promoting National Products

— Sun Choucheng

The manuscript "Talking about Cotton Flannel Shirts at Nanhu Lake" by Tianran Jun in this journal cannot help but remind me of the humorous history of buying cold-weather clothing in the vicinity of Yuanyang Lake, where I was compelled to do so by the Wind Aunt and Rain Master. It concerns the promotion of national products, therefore I will record the events of that day in this journal, which I trust is what fellow comrades who are enthusiastic about promoting national products also wish to hear. This year, the Yousheng Travel Group initiated a moon viewing at Nanhu Lake. After the evening banquet at the Yanyu Tower, there were more than 300 participants. My colleagues Sun Mingqi and his wife from the National Association of Pharmaceutical Industry Trade Unions were both among them. Mr. Sun sent me a train ticket because I am originally from Jiaxing, and am more familiar with the famous sights of Hezhong, inviting me to go with him. The kindness of a friend is weighty, and difficult to refuse, so at 7:00 a.m. that morning I went to the station. After the wheel started, I saw Ren Shigang, the manager of the Wuhe Weaving Factory, Fang Jiange, the manager of the Zhonghua Enamel Factory, and Xu Yangnan, the manager of the Hongxin Cloth Factory, and their wives, all there. After exchanging greetings, Mr. Fang said that Mr. Pan Yangyao had originally intended to come, but was unable to do so due to business, so his daughter, Ms. Shi Quan, represented him. He pointed to Ms. Pan and introduced her to me. After a brief chat, I learned that she was working at the Four Banks Savings Society. Her demeanor was generous, and her words were elegant, which showed that she came from a family with a long academic tradition, different from the rest. A tiger father does not beget a dog son, truly. After arriving in He, we first visited the Railway Nursery, where many chrysanthemums were planted, but unfortunately it was too early and none of them were in bloom. Then we went to the Dongta Temple to pay respects to the tomb of Zhu Maichen. There were few cars and many people, and the Jiao Li Street was suddenly crowded. The tomb is located north of the tower, behind my old house. In the midst of overgrown weeds and desolate smoke, there is a stone tablet standing upright. People all stepped through the weeds to gaze at it, all saying that if there were no Peking opera of "Water Splashed Before the Horse," the public would not value this person so much. Therefore, his fame was actually created by his wife, Cui. At 11:00 a.m., we boarded a boat to the Yanyu Tower, some went to the Baomei Pavilion to appreciate the plums painted by Peng Gangzhi, and others went to the Leizu Temple to visit the images of Guanshiyin, etc. After lunch, we went to the Three Pagodas to see the Blood Imprint Monk. Midway, the wind and rain mingled, and the weather suddenly turned cold. Upon arriving at the Chachan Temple, everyone showed signs of shivering. After I told them that the Blood Imprint Monk was a resident monk of the Chachan Temple, named Miaodi, and that during the Jiajing period of the Ming Dynasty, the Japanese pirates occupied the Southeast, took women and children hostage, and detained them in this temple. Miaodi heard the crying and was moved by the thought of Bodhi. He got the guards drunk and released them all. After the guards woke up, they hated him to the bone, tied him to the stone archway, and burned him to death with piled firewood, and the shadow appeared. It has been hundreds of years now, and it has not receded. In the 15th year of the Republic of China, when Wei Daofeng was the magistrate of Jiaxing, he admired his loyalty and righteousness, and specially erected a monument to praise him. After the facts, the public was suddenly enlightened. Because it concerned national character, everyone showed a righteous face, as if they were wrapped in cotton, and did not feel cold. At 3:00 p.m., we went around the West City to the Shanqing Gate. The weather was even colder. Approaching the city, everyone went to Tangwan Street to buy cotton flannel shirts to resist the cold. I told my fellow boaters that the market was full of foreign goods, and that they should pay special attention to this. Among domestic products, the Goose brand of Wuhe is the most famous and can be tried. Everyone agreed. After buying them, all the shirts were printed with a goose. I turned to Mr. Wang and said, "If your ancestor Mr. Yi Zhi was here today, I wonder how he would dance and stomp for this kind of Goose brand cotton flannel shirt." Everyone laughed heartily. At the evening banquet at the Yanyu Tower, Chang'e hid and did not come out, and the Rain Master and Wind Aunt still displayed their power, causing the silk sleeves to feel cold. Fortunately, we relied on this cotton flannel shirt to resist, otherwise it would have been difficult to support. Therefore, there was much goodwill towards the Wuhe Weaving Factory. Mr. Ren and his wife smiled. Some people who did not manage to buy cotton flannel shirts used the towels of the Sanyou Industrial Society as scarves.

It is heard that the Nanjing Road East Asia Hotel United Promotion Market has this brush on display for promotion.

In order for all sectors to understand the excellence of the car tire, the factory has printed a large number of brochures. Send a letter to request one.

New National Product Oilcloth (Double Hammer Brand)

Architect Mr. Cao Kedong, a native of Shanghai, is dedicated to studying architecture. In the early years of the Republic of China, he was employed by the Tianjin French Engineering Bureau, where he served for nearly 20 years. Most of the famous buildings in major cities in North China rely on his planning. Mr. Cao is especially fond of studying building materials, such as organizing the Yudong Brick and Tile Company and the Kaiming Electric Company, and has achieved remarkable results. Recently, in the building materials, oilcloth is a product that has no domestic output, and all of them need to use foreign goods. The outflow of money is a pity! He has carefully studied its raw materials and ingredients, and has built his own special oilcloth machine without borrowing external force. After more than three years of painstaking research, he organized the Jianhua Oilcloth Company last summer and manufactured several types of fully national product oilcloth with the double hammer brand. All provinces in North China have already adopted it. They all believe that the quality is excellent and can surpass imported products, and the pricing is extremely low. It has now been registered and filed with the Ministry of Industry and has been granted trademark exclusive rights. This time, in response to the exhibition of national product building materials, there are many samples for the reference of major architects, in order to promote national products and regain rights.
