Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Tianxu Wosheng)

Don't complain about the heat. If you compare yourself with the people who farm the land, you will feel calm and realize that you are really too impatient.

A minister's heart is like water. Comparing the heart to water is the most appropriate. It is better for the heart to be cold than hot, because when it gets close to the boiling point, it will be tormented and gasified, until it is scorched and dried. If you don't want it to be tormented, it is also very easy. Just take it away from the fire and it will cool down.

The coldness and heat of the human heart are the same as the coldness and heat of water. There is less due to heaven and more due to man. Throughout the year, it is really rare for it to be hot to C氏38 degrees and cold to 0 degrees. As the saying goes, the great cold does not last more than three days, and the great heat does not last more than three days, which shows that among the 365 days of the year, there are only these six days. It can be said that it is extremely rare. However, human power can overcome heaven. He uses coal fire to torment, and sucks with air to force, and can immediately make water gasified into the ocean. Isn't this man-made?

Those who have the thought of starting hotness are mostly people who are full and warm and are not satisfied. If you make that person feel the oppression of hunger and cold, and seek to avoid freezing and starvation, he will run and shout under the scorching sun. Even if he sweats profusely and feels like he's burning inside, he will never want to resist this annoyance with lightning, wind, and cold air.

Military Food for Italian Troops Stationed in Africa

— Pei Yu

Amidst the tense atmosphere of preparing to kick off the Italo-Abyssinian War, two types of merchants are making a fortune. The first type making a big fortune is the arms dealer, the second type making a small fortune is the water and vegetable merchant. The arms dealer's big customer is Abyssinia, and the water and vegetable merchant's big customer is Italy. Abyssinia cannot manufacture arms themselves, so they must procure them from abroad. The arms dealers have already calculated this big business and cannot escape it. But the transaction of water and vegetables for Italy, the water and vegetable merchants had not expected, it really is "extra money" business. Italy procured a large number of lemons and oranges, and transported them to the Italian colonies in Eritrea and Somaliland, to be used as provisions for the troops stationed in Africa.

Italian soldiers stationed in Somaliland are given three oranges or lemons per person per day, but Italian soldiers in Eritrea are given one serving of this fruit every two days. Because the terrain of Eritrea is higher than that of Somaliland, and the climate is more suitable for hygiene, the need for water and vegetables is relatively small, so the amount of fruit in the military food is slightly reduced. This fruit is very beneficial to the health of troops in tropical areas; especially lemons, which are extremely necessary, are an indispensable savior in the epidemic of typhoid fever.

In addition to fruit, each person is also given one and a half pounds of bread, six to nine ounces of meat, six ounces of macaroni, three and a half ounces of potatoes, two ounces of vegetables, and one ounce of tobacco per day. Twice a week, macaroni is replaced with the same amount of rice. In addition, the army also supplies a small amount of seasoning, oil, cheese, and one and a half ounces of jam every day. Italian soldiers in Eritrea are also given half an ounce of coffee and three-quarters of an ounce of sugar per day; Italian soldiers in Somaliland are given twice as much per day.

Long Rainbow Studio Painting Notes

— Zheng Yimei

Master Shanfu Shengtan said: "After dancing, one wants to soak in the reeds and play the flute, but the hands tremble severely; after playing loud brass instruments, one wants to play the serene xiao flute, but the ears ring terribly; after galloping on horseback, one wants to enter the ranks and dance, but one is severely out of breath; after scolding the audience, one wants to chant Buddhist hymns, but one's throat is terribly dry." Unexpectedly, what the ancients found difficult, modern people can handle with ease, as if it were nothing. Their talent is truly astonishing! My friend, Mr. Xie Xian'ou, along with the three elders, Shen Xinhai, Jin Suixiang, and Zhu Liangcai, and the gentlemen Ren Changnian, Chen Zhuting, and Li Pangen, formed the Long Rainbow Studio in Hejia Branch Lane on Shangwen Road, enjoying painting as their daily pleasure. Yesterday, I visited them and saw Mr. Xie was painting a "Snail Shell Taoist Temple" on a fan surface. On the side of a hillside, two old men sat, leisurely watching a snail's opening and closing. Due to the size ratio, the snail only occupied a corner of the fan surface. Inside the shell, several generations of monks were performing Buddhist rituals, with scriptures, cushions, incense, flowers, offerings, and the light of the initiation of the bodhisattva. Other items such as tables, benches, bells, drums, gongs, and cymbals were all present. Two lamp stands stood tall in front of the door, and banners fluttered. Using a magnifying glass to examine it, every detail was discernible, without a single careless stroke. It was truly marvelous. Looking around, I saw a large figure hanging on the wall, displaying a radiant spirit and an open composition. The power of the brushstrokes was unparalleled. Compared to the one large and one small of the "Snail Shell" painting, it was as if they were from two different hands. Upon closer inspection, the colors were not yet dry. Mr. Xie stopped his work and discussed figure painting with me, saying, "Figure paintings mostly depict stories and poetic ideas. However, houses, tables, chairs, carriages, clothes, and decorations change with each era. The artist must study the era and incorporate it into the painting. The background, whether it's a tree or a stone, should complement the ups, downs, turns, and sides. The composition should be simple but not desolate, dense but not chaotic, distinguishing between the front and back, so that the distance is naturally apparent. The distance must be measured in inches, and the height must establish a host and guests, so there is no imbalance or overweighting." He also said, "When engaging in painting, one should concentrate all of one's spirit, with the idea preceding the brush, so that the brushstrokes are naturally vigorous and smooth." All of these are words of gained experience, which students of painting should regard as rules. Mr. Xie showed me landscape and flower paintings by the three elders and Chen Zhuting, Chen Ya, Jin Zhuozhuo, Li Pangen, and Zhou Xiaona, all full of ancient charm. I enjoyed them for a long time. I heard that the gentlemen have recently been very enthusiastic and are planning to form a calligraphy and painting society with people in society.

— Juanyin

After a year of separation, I came to the window again today, unable to bear watching the continuous disasters.

Little Western Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 19: An Official Cherishes His Reputation and Knocks on the Door with Skill; New Love Separates Flesh and Blood; Visiting the Sick Is Impossible

You are older than me, you are like my own brother. When an own brother asks his younger brother to do something, why would he need to be polite? You can just order me around. If you don't ask me to do something, it means you think I'm not good enough, and don't want this good-for-nothing as a friend." Duocai was put in an awkward position by his words, and was embarrassed to not ask him for help, so he cupped his hands and said, "In that case, I'll have to trouble you." Shi Lian didn't wait for a second word, and quickly walked towards the back door of Little Western Heaven. Before he even reached Aunt Hu's house, just seeing her front door, he was startled. An old woman as thin as a skeleton was sitting on her front door frame, leaning against the wall. The blue cloth jacket on her body had at least twenty or thirty patches, large and small. She had her legs crossed, and her blue cloth pants were covered in yellow dirt. Her pointed face had yellow-black skin covered in wrinkles, her eyes were sunken, her two cheekbones stuck out, and silvery hair covered her face. In addition, her lifeless eyes were fixedly staring at the back of Little Western Heaven, making her particularly frightening. Therefore, she stood from afar. But that old woman did not forgive people for being afraid of her, and raised a hand like a chicken claw, extending two fingers, pointing at Shi Lian, and slowly said: "Old man, aren't you from Little Western Heaven? Have you seen my Yueying? I'm sick. Alas! I... miss... her." Shi Lian then knew that she was Yueying's grandmother. Since she had spoken, she was a person, and there was no need to be so afraid of her, so he slowly approached her and asked: "Old woman, are you asking about the mistress of the house?" The old woman looked up at him, clasped her palms and bowed twice, tremblingly saying: "Old man, I am a person about to die. I am old enough to die. What is the point of living such a bitter life? My two generations, that little bit of flesh and blood, were sold for a hundred dollars. I... really don't want to... him. His mother, how could she bear to sell him? But we live with relatives, and the relatives are also poor..." (331)

Records of Imperial Incense Drifting

— Original by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

(No chapters listed) Meeting of the Author and Translator

Just as my translation of "Records of Imperial Incense Drifting" was nearing completion, suddenly, like a storm, the original author of the book, "Princess Der Ling," arrived (the title of Princess may still be in question, but until she officially corrects it, I can only continue to use it). In the past few days, various Chinese and Western newspapers in Shanghai have been publishing her actions and conversations. Indeed, since the publication of "Records of Imperial Incense Drifting," this name, which was about to be forgotten, has received the attention of many people again; and she happened to return to her homeland at the right time, so it is no wonder that so many people went to the Cathay Hotel to see her, even to the point where she felt overwhelmed.

The news of her arrival naturally brought me a special kind of excitement, because although I had translated her work so meticulously and gained an understanding of her as a woman full of courage and very fond of joking, I had never directly met her. Since it was difficult for me to go to America to find her, then I would definitely have to see her now that she had come here. But unfortunately, I have been unusually busy lately, and because I suffer from insomnia, I have to rest after eight o'clock in the evening. As a result, I don't have any suitable time to visit this Americanized Chinese lady. Furthermore, one day I accidentally read the North-China Daily News and saw a report about her, which included a very absurd statement, roughly saying that "Princess Der Ling is now a woman without a nationality, since the Qing Dynasty has perished, she has lost her qualification as a Chinese citizen..." I don't know if these words are from the North-China Daily News reporter who lacks common sense, or if they are from this Americanized lady? But no matter what, it made me very unhappy; I don't dare to boast about how patriotic I am, but I would have to sincerely and respectfully visit someone who is clearly a citizen of the Republic of China, but prefers to be a foreigner, that is something I'm unwilling to do, so things have been delayed. Small Knowledge

— (Chuyu)

Knowledge for Distinguishing Butter Butter is rich in nutrition, but in recent years, there have been many fake products on the market, such as artificial butter masquerading as pure butter, so we should carefully distinguish the quality. Artificial butter is made of synthetic milk and various other fats, with very few nutrients and vitamins, and the smell is also different. The method of distinguishing is to cut a piece of butter with a knife, spread it on bread, and bake it over a fire. If it is of pure quality, then there will definitely be fine bubbles rising, and after the oil dissolves, it will turn yellow. If it is artificial butter, then there will be very few fine bubbles, and there will be a popping sound. After the oil dissolves, white grease will congeal on top.

Eating Milk Requires Avoiding Acidic Products If lemon, orange, or other acidic fruit juices are mixed into milk, then the acid will react with the protein in the milk and coagulate. Eating this milk can cause indigestion in mild cases and poisoning in severe cases.

Do Not Use Linen Cloth to Wipe Glasses If you use a linen or silk handkerchief to wipe them, it will damage the lenses and change the light of the lenses. Also, when taking off your glasses, do not let the convex surface of the lens touch the tabletop. You should support the lenses with the temples or place them facing upwards. It is certainly appropriate to use a velvet cloth to wipe the lenses, but if the velvet cloth is used for too long, it will be the same as linen cloth. It is best to use thin pieces of paper (eyeglass paper) to wipe them.

Preventing Soot from Forming on the Bottom of Pots The bottom of rice pots and vegetable pots will inevitably accumulate black soot from burning wood to cook things. To prevent this, you can first soak the bottom of the pot in water and then rub it with soap. In that case, the soot will dissolve due to the soap and will not easily thicken. If you wash it with water, the soot will also fall off easily. This saves much more effort than using a knife to scrape off the soot.

The Use of Cigarette Butts Do not throw away the cigarette butts left over from smoking. Collect them in a bucket and soak them in water, because the nicotine in the butts will dissolve in the water. Then, filter it out with gauze. This liquid can be sprinkled in gutters or trash cans to prevent pests from breeding. Also, dipping a brush in this liquid and applying it to the branches and leaves of plants can kill scale insects. This is truly waste utilization, killing two birds with one stone.

Precautions When Wearing Shoes Barefoot When wearing shoes barefoot, you should first pad the soles with blotting paper, and then line them with thin cloth. In that case, the foot sweat will be absorbed by the blotting paper, and the soles of the feet can be kept clean. If there is a lot of dead skin on the soles of the feet, it is easiest to soil shoes and socks. You should scrape it off with a bamboo chip after washing your feet. New socks, because they have starch, should be washed with warm water first, and then they can be worn.

Disinfecting the Odor in Toilets To remove the odor from toilets, copper sulfate, potassium permanganate, and camphor are generally used. Other oils such as camphor oil, Abous, and Alis-Taihin all have bactericidal effects. If you scatter camphor balls in the toilet and put naphthalene balls in the urinal, you can avoid foul odors and deodorize, which is more effective than the odor-removing liquids sold on the market.

Writing Method on Metal Utensils If you want to write or draw on metal utensils, first apply wax to the surface, and carve with a needle. The wax is removed by the needle, leaving holes. Then, pour sulfuric acid or hydrochloric acid into the carved holes, leave it for several hours, and then wash away the acid with water. After scraping off the wax, the written or drawn parts will be corroded by the acid.

Preventing Mirrors and Glass from Fogging When the weather is cold, indoor mirrors and glass will fog up due to water vapor. The methods to prevent this are as follows: 1. Rub with dry tobacco. 2. Mix half Kresalgin and half clean water, and wipe the mirror surface with a cloth. 3. Add 10% Kresalgin to wood alcohol, first apply it with a cloth, and then wipe it clean with a dry cloth. All of these are effective.

Correction The article "Literacy Movement" published in the September 23rd issue was written by me. The original manuscript was signed by Wang Shapa. I don't know why it was attributed to Mr. Zhi Yanbo Guang? The issue of article remuneration is a minor matter, but there are some discrepancies involving my wife Lanxin and my young daughter Yanhong, so I hope you will investigate and correct them. Thank you. Wang Shapa

Free Talk

A Supplement on the Theory of Tea Drinking Literature

— Tang Tao

In his Night Voyage Collection, Mr. Aying has an article dedicated to tea drinking, called "On the Theory of Tea Drinking Literature." He points out that tea drinking is an elegant affair for hermits and celebrities, and it is also their privilege. He also explains the boredom of the so-called "entrusting sorrows to bitter tea," and cites extensively, making it a good article that uses the past as a mirror to the present.

Because this question is very interesting, I would also like to talk about it. Why is it called a supplement? That is to say, I want to talk about something that Mr. Aying has not talked about in detail—or even the dross that he despises.

First of all, let's talk about tea drinking. Don't rough people get thirsty after work? It's true that they want to drink tea, but they only know how to drink, but they never thought that they could also eat it. Using a covered bowl, a purple sand teapot, sipping and chewing carefully, paying attention to taste, paying attention to fragrance, and even paying attention to color, these are all the privileges of elegant people, and rough men can't share them. So tea drinking also becomes literature, and it is elegant literature.

It is said that tea leaves were first used as a beverage in the Tang Dynasty, but some say it was in the Jin Dynasty. The Tea Record says: "Tea was not eaten in ancient times. Since the Jin Dynasty, the Wu people have picked the leaves and boiled them, called tea porridge." However, the literature of tea drinking was in the Tang Dynasty anyway. In addition to Lu Yu's (Hongjian) Tea Classic and Lu Tong's (Wangchuanzi) Tea Song, Bai Letian, Liu Yuxi and others also have poems and articles to record it. However, these articles were quite looked down upon by the people of the Song Dynasty because of the progress of tea drinking literature. Yuan Zhifu (Wen) said:

Liu Mengde's tea poem says: "Pick it yourself next to the fragrant bushes, and stir-fry it into a full room of fragrance." From this, we know that the Tang people were not good at drinking tea. If he saw the wonderful works of Cai Junmo and Ding Wei of this dynasty, then he would not write poetry. The freshly picked tea must be fragrant, and its fragrance should be twice that of ordinary tea, not comparable to dragon musk. The ancients used dragon musk in tea, which damaged the tea a lot; tea has a natural fragrance, so why should it be fake to dragon musk! Huang Taishi's poem says: "If you want to grind a cup of new fragrance, you shouldn't pass on treasures to come from the clouds." It is known that the fragrance of new tea is especially lovely. "He also commented on Bai Letian's tea poem and said:

Bai Yaotian's tea poem says: "嘗一 綠昌明", Changming is a place name in Mianzhou, and people say that Changming tea is green, which is not true! This is similar to the sentence "Green dust flies beside the golden grinding plate". It is because he did not know how to make tea at that time, and the production was not fine, so the color of the tea was still green. And the好事者 recorded the beauty of the tea, and did not value white, so his poem is like this. If Letian saw the beauty of today's tea, would he be willing to say this!

The Cai Junmo and Ding Wei (Gongyan) mentioned by Zhifu are two famous tea drinking literati in the Song Dynasty. Su Dongpo's poem says: "粟粒芽 beside the Wuyi stream, with Ding and Cai and cage added before and after." Also said these two. Ding Gongyan wrote a tea picture, and Cai Junmo wrote a tea record.

Mr. Aying described the tea drinking literature of the Ming Dynasty in great detail in "On the Theory of Tea Drinking Literature," so there is no need to repeat it here. However, since Wang Mengduan passed Wuxi, visited Huishan, entered Ting Song'an, and built a bamboo stove, everyone who visited Huiquan had to write a few poems. During the Qing Dynasty, there were dozens of families including Li Dongyang. These poems are all collected behind the Ming Dynasty printed tea making new book reprinted during the Guangxu period.

The method of tea drinking became more and more advanced in the Qing Dynasty, but that literature was not as good as that of the predecessors. For example, in the tea making new book, I personally think that the works of the Qing Dynasty are far inferior to those before the Qing Dynasty. For example, Yong Shuangjing Tea Yun:

In a place where people cannot reach the wind and sun, the Supreme Jade Hall is full of treasures. I can imagine Dongpo, an old recluse, waving his pen and pouring out hundreds of hu of bright pearls. My family in Jiangnan picks Yunyu, 落 纷纷雪不如. I will wake up the dream of Huangzhou for you and return to the lake in a flat boat.

Although this consciousness is still the old consciousness of the traditional tea drinking literati, and there is no creation, but if you talk about words, it is really much better than those who deliberately carve. For example, Lu Tong's Tea Song not only said:

... Yuchuanzi, take this clear wind to go back, the group of immortals on the mountain are in charge of the land, the status is clear and high, separated by wind and rain, how can you know that hundreds of millions of creatures suffer with cliffs? Ask the common people from Jian Ji again, can they get respite in the end?

Can a great work that specializes in helping poetry and boosting literary thoughts be said to be better than this? Drinking tea without forgetting the tea pickers is really a branch of tea drinking literature.

The current bitter tea faction has nothing to do with this other branch, because they still want to be secluded and elegant, which is the authentic orthodoxy. I remember that Fengshi Wenjianji recorded the story of Lu Hongjian, the tea ancestor:

Li Jiqing was sent to comfort Jiangnan, and tea drinking was becoming popular at that time. Lu Yu came to see him. After sitting down, he cooked tea himself, and talked about the names of the tea, distinguishing and pointing out. Duke Li looked down on him in his heart. After the tea was over, he ordered the slave to take thirty Wen to pay the tea doctor.

Although this seems to spoil the scenery, it is still pleasant to treat those tea children and tea grandchildren who specialize in elegance.

Novels of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom

— Han Feng

Beyond the *Taiping Heavenly Kingdom Trimetrical Classic*, the most important item in this unique manuscript is a novel about the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom. Everyone discusses the poetry and prose of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, but obviously little has been said about novels, naturally due to the scarcity of materials. The Taiping Heavenly Kingdom did have its own novels. What were the content and form of their novels? This article provides some hints. Its foundation remains built on religion, "mythologizing" all "human affairs." The novel is titled "True Account of the Origins of the Uprising," with the subtitle "Newly Engraved in the Third Year of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom." The character "Quan" in Xiuquan's name is written as "泉," avoiding the Heavenly King's taboo. The author's surname is Zeng, but the given name is unknown. In the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, this novel should occupy a significant position. Its content describes the history of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom's uprising and explains the meaning of the uprising. The full text is less than two thousand words, and I present it again to readers as valuable, initial historical material of Taiping Heavenly Kingdom culture.

"True Account of the Origins of the Uprising, Newly Engraved in the Third Year of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom"

Zeng said: Mencius said that a true king arises every five hundred years. From Hongwu until now, more than five hundred years have passed, and the rise of a true king is at hand. In the third year of Shunzhi, Zhu's descendants of Taichang settled in Liushuwan of Guohua, and today there are only a few dozen families. To the west of the bay is Chaxiang Ridge. In the first year of Daoguang, Mr. Lin Qing from Henan built a thatched hut on the side of the ridge and lived there. He called himself the Chaxiao Recluse, and he could observe qi, predict fortune and misfortune, and was always accurate. He once told someone, "Auspicious qi rises from the Zhu Bay, and great nobility will surely emerge." On the eighteenth day of the fourth month of the sixth year [of Daoguang], Zhu Fan dreamt at night that a divine being rode a yellow dragon past Liushuwan, preceded by two boys as guides. She awoke with a start and abdominal pain, giving birth to a son. That night, a red light shone in the western sky, visible far and wide, and no one could fathom its origin. I, Zeng, live on Laoya Slope, three miles from Liushuwan. I was forty-seven years old, and that night my wife also gave birth, delivering twin boys. Three days later, I heard about the Fan family's dream and was surprised. I went to inquire with Mr. Chaxiao. The master was unwilling to speak openly. After repeated inquiries, he instructed me not to leak the divine secret. He whispered to me, "The one riding the yellow dragon past Liushuwan is the incarnation of Jesus. The two boys are the incarnations of Yuntan and Yunfan. Rejection of evil and return to the right will occur after the fish and turtles dwell in the mountains." In the sixth year, the Zhu family invited my two sons to study with Mr. Chaxiao. The master was versed in the writings of Confucius and Mencius and knowledgeable in the military strategies of Sun Tzu and Wu Qi. He taught the classics earnestly by day and military strategy at night. The students were extraordinarily quick-witted. Over ten years, they made academic achievements. Someone asked the master, "Those who succeed in learning will surely achieve fame. The students have achieved great success, but why do they not pursue fame and fortune?" The master smiled without answering. On the ninth day of the ninth month of the twenty-first year [of Daoguang], the master invited me to climb the ridge peak. We sat on a boulder, looked up at the celestial phenomena, and he pointed out the positions of the stars, saying, "This one will rise, and that one will fall." I listened silently. He pointed again, saying, "Black qi fills the northwest, and fish and turtles will dwell in the mountains." He advised me to move. I was reluctant to leave my hometown, but he did not move. On the jiazi day of the eleventh month, the master dismissed the students and burned down the thatched hut at night, disappearing without a trace. The following year, there was indeed a great flood, and the mountains and plains were submerged. For eight years, the imperial court did not provide disaster relief, and the county imposed penalties for resisting taxes. The people who fled, died, and were wiped out are countless. Hong Xi'en of Changle Village in Zhongxiang was a good man. His two sons, the elder son Xiuquan, was versed in military strategy and was once recommended as a cultured and filial scholar. The younger son, Xiuzhen, was both wise and brave and was once recommended as a martial and filial scholar. His family was as wealthy as Tao Zhu and surpassed Cheng Luo in wealth. In the face of this great disaster, he generously gave aid. Countless people in the county, supporting the old and carrying the young, flocked to the Hong family seeking relief. I, along with Zhu, led my two sons to visit him, and we talked all day, as if we were old acquaintances. We were invited to stay at the Shangzhi Hall in the Fuyuan Garden. The county magistrate, Wen Keyao, held a grudge against Xi'en for refusing to lend him money. He accused him of seeking to win over the hearts of the people, arrested Xi'en and imprisoned him, and sent soldiers to escort him to the provincial authorities. The entire county refused to submit and ambushed and killed dozens of government soldiers on the road. Civil and military officials sent urgent reports, and troops were dispatched to carry out arrests throughout the county. Xi cried, "For the sake of my family, the entire county will be harmed. I cannot bear it. Quickly bind me and my son and send us to the prefect to save the lives of the entire county." Zhu said, "No, things have come to this, there is no use in acting like children. When our teacher, Mr. Lin Qing, set up his school on Chaxiao Ridge, he said: When fish and turtles dwell in the mountains, the people will suffer terribly. Before the affairs of Jiuli, a blood oath is sworn with sacrificial animals. West of Guohua, north of Hongdou. Heroes gather like clouds, and the oath is jointly sworn. Now it has come true. I have heard that in Guangdong Province there is Wanding Mountain, which stretches for over a hundred li and is very steep. Heroes gather there and have established four kings. The Eastern King, Yang Junfu, the Western King, Xiao Jicheng, the Southern King, Qian Shaoyao, and the Northern King, He Youdong, all have the talent to govern the world. They have brave men under their command, numbering over ten thousand. My friend, Guo Wannian of Jingxi, has communicated with the four kings. Please take this matter to them, and it will surely succeed. I and Brother Xiu will unite the respected scholars and righteous men of the entire county, eliminate corrupt officials and greedy bureaucrats, confiscate all the records of Guohua, and wait for the heroes to gather and dominate Guangxi. We will assess the situation, deploy troops, and store grain, straddling Guangdong and Guangxi, and sweeping through Hubei. We will control Jiujiang and march straight down, dividing into five armies to drive forward. The people of Jiangnan will surely be terrified by the news, lacking the wisdom to plan and the courage to act. Taking Nanjing will be as easy as shaking off withered leaves. From then on, we will use Nanjing as our base, pacifying them if they are compliant and conquering them if they resist. In less than ten years, the world will be settled. Why cling to petty faith and minor details, and head towards danger and destruction, fulfilling the desires of the fox and dog party?" Xi was delighted and said, "Zhu's words are correct. Today, it is you who will ruin your family and sacrifice your body, and it is you who will transform your family into a nation." Thus, they recruited brave men from far and wide, not even speaking, they had already over ten thousand people. In front of Jiuli Pavilion, they swore an oath of blood together. The crowd pushed Xi to be the leader of the alliance. Xi said, "I am old! There is Zhu present!" The corrupt officials and greedy bureaucrats have all been killed. Guo called for the heroes to gather at Wanding. Again, they swore an oath of blood, and Xi was still appointed as the leader of the alliance. Xi again said, "There is Zhu present!" The kings were all sincerely convinced. This happened in the third month of the twenty-ninth year [of Daoguang]. I remember the words of Lin Qing, Mr. Xiaoguang, were truly the foresight of the master, and they have proven accurate to this day. But where is the master, that he does not participate in this alliance? I deeply regret it. I want to magnify the master's name and write this record."

The author of this text has considerable literary talent. As recorded, aside from the mythological parts, all are actual events, which will bring about many changes to our past known thoughts and facts. And what is particularly noteworthy is that the author is making every effort to promote "Zhu Sheng," and says very little about Xiuquan. From the lines between the words, it seems that he is quite indignant for "Zhu Sheng." Thus, the internal contradictions of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom in the early stages, the news of which can be seen in this. But who is this "Zhu Sheng"? What is meant by "first first thing," generally spoken, "smoke bomb" only.

Fellow Villagers (Continued)

— Hei Ying

This fellow villager of mine was very good at speaking. He even carried a deck of Holland cards and was quite skilled at playing. But I didn't feel any interest in him. "Then let's talk about something," he pushed the cards towards his wicker basket.

"Little brother," he began calling me that. "You're still young and very naive! For example, gambling with Holland cards, you're not my match. If you have five hundred, you'll lose five hundred, not even a penny will be left! You know I've traveled all over the British and Dutch territories, made friends with big bosses, and scratched out two hundred dollars playing mahjong in Chinese associations!" His eyebrows rose, and he touched his chin, where coarse black whiskers grew.

I didn't say anything, letting him continue: "How many years have you been away from ××? I left when I was nineteen, and only went back last winter. ×× is not like it used to be: roads, cars, movie theaters, and prostitutes—guess what they're like? Naturally, they're better than the native women in Batavia or Singapore. Clean and tidy, at least they won't give you syphilis... What's wrong, little brother? You're carrying on like a young virgin who's never touched a woman's flesh!"

I felt uneasy in front of this worldly man. He was talking about things that Genwu had never mentioned to me, although Genwu was perhaps even more experienced than him. He seemed very clever, and when he discovered that I wasn't interested in women, he immediately changed the subject:

"I forgot to ask you, what are you going to Medan to do?"

"Me? Someone introduced me to a minor position at the Chamber of Commerce there."

"That's good, little brother, a minor position—young people, how can they become secretaries or chairmen right after leaving their thatched huts? And do you know the current situation, what they call: recession! There are so many unemployed people. You're very lucky!" He leaned against the half-old leather suitcase and finished speaking, sometimes staring at me. When he smiled, I could see his teeth that had turned black.

Having a fellow villager on the journey who liked to talk did indeed break the loneliness of a single traveler. But I never understood what kind of person he was. Several times I tried to ask him, but he cleverly evaded the questions. Once he even said this:

"Little brother, what are you worried about! With someone as honest and reliable as you, I must promote you. Wait until you get to Medan, and I'll give you a not-so-small position."

But what I saw was a not-so-wealthy steerage passenger, just like me, with only two pieces of luggage and the shirt he was wearing seemed to have not been changed for a long time, with stains all over the collar and back. He smoked cheap cigarettes; even once when I was walking with him past a place that sold cigarettes, he asked me if I had money for two packs of Elephant Brand cigarettes.

"I don't know when my small change was used up. Give it to me, little brother. We must talk about fellow villager feelings."

Using the fine-sounding term of fellow villager feelings, this self-proclaimed elder took the money for his cigarettes from my dry pocket. While smoking, he said to me:

"For the sake of fellow villager feelings, I will definitely take good care of you. Tomorrow morning the ship will enter Belawan, and from there you can take a car to Medan."

In this way, he wanted my luggage to be placed with his, to go ashore together. When I handed him the leather suitcase, his hand kept touching it, and he exclaimed:

"Good stuff! Worth ten dollars of goods!"

The ship stopped at Belawan. I followed the colonial government's disembarkation procedures to the immigration office to report. The fellow villager and the luggage waited for me outside, because he was an old customer, he only needed to present his residence permit for inspection and it was done. The head of the immigration office, while staring at my face with his deep blue eyes, searched for words to interrogate me. In this way, a full half hour passed, and like releasing a prisoner, I was let out. Outside, there were many cars, carriages, and people walking around. I looked for that fellow villager, but there was no sign of him!

In the letter to Genwu, I wrote:

"Genwu: I arrived here safely, but the luggage is gone. It's not finally because I don't know anyone, I met a very fellow villagerly ×× person on the ship. But this fellow villager has now disappeared along with my luggage..." (The End)

Night Scene of the City

— Tong Qinglan

This boundless night wind

Shakes the brass bell in front of the rickshaw,

Mixed in with the motorcycle horn,

Sharply piercing through the heart of the street;

Sweat squeezed out,

Mixed with the dust underfoot,

On the smooth floor,

Whiskey mixes messily;

Thin, bony hands

Pull the wheels forward,

Soft, fat arms

Drag tender, white flesh to roll;

Sand fills empty stomachs,

The roadside ditch

Flows with fermented leftovers;

This deathly still world

Is filled with dimness,

This night scene will continue until dawn.

Written in Xiamen, 1935

Honorable Old Woman (1)

— Written by Jiang Ma Xiu, Translated by Ren Gou

Recently, I just wanted to see Chaplin's "Kid," so we ran into a suburban movie theater. However, the delightful "Kid" had already been half shown and was about to end. Next, the famous military propaganda film "Colonel Yoshioka" began. I felt very disappointed and planned to go back immediately, but having spent money to specially run in here, it was inevitably a pity to go out like this.

"Hey, what do you think? Do you want to continue watching?" I asked my wife who came with me.

"Well," she hesitated: "But we have already come specially, so let's watch another one. I haven't seen Japanese movies for a long time, so it's okay to watch one occasionally."

"But, 'Colonel Yoshioka'..."

"That doesn't matter. Let's see what military propaganda films are like and use it as a reference."

"What you said also makes sense."

So I sat down and continued to watch "Colonel Yoshioka," which was starting on the screen.

My wife and I haven't watched Japanese movies at all in the past few years. Past disappointments simply didn't allow us to have the mood to watch Japanese movies. But now, as we watched "Colonel Yoshioka," first of all, we felt admiration and felt that Japanese movies had also greatly improved. The development of the plot was very natural, without exaggeration. The selection of each scene and the methods of photography were also very clever. The actors also performed enthusiastically and skillfully. The humor shown in various places was also quite effective, very suitable for the audience's tastes. In particular, what was shown in the film was the Japanese life that we were in, everything was very cordial and could be deeply felt. Even the performances that made people laugh were not like watching Chaplin's movies, feeling that they were things that were far away from us; on the contrary, they could make people feel vividly that they were really very close to us and very consistent with the situation. The film slowly played on, and the crowd filled in the theater gradually became enthusiastic. To be honest, even we finally watched quite enthusiastically.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

The Increase in Crime

— Xiong Cheng

Previously saw the newspaper report: "According to the Public Concession Bureau Police Department's August report: The number of reported criminal cases this month totaled 1,422, an increase of 29% compared to July, and also an increase of 34 cases compared to the same month last year; the number of criminals arrested this month also increased compared to the previous figures, totaling 1,374 people... If we speak of the types of crimes separately, there was one murder case and one attempted murder case in August. There were a total of nineteen robbery cases this month, sixteen ordinary theft cases, and thirty-seven house theft cases..."

In Shanghai, China, the Public Concession of Shanghai (excluding the French Concession and the Chinese territory), in the month of August alone, there were 1,422 criminal cases "reported," and 1,374 criminals were arrested. Compared with the same month last year and the previous month of this year, there has been an increase. This is truly "enough to be alarming."

If we calculate the total number of cases in all of Shanghai, within twelve months, and those not "reported," what a huge number it will be. If we speak of the whole of China, what a huge number it will be!

Undoubtedly, the large number of criminal cases completely reflects the extent to which the current economic recession in Chinese society has deepened. At the same time, from the statement "an increase of thirty-four cases compared to the same month last year...an increase of twenty-nine cases compared to July," it can be seen that the recession is deepening rapidly!

However, what is the reason for this phenomenon? Obviously, this is definitely not because of "people's hearts not being as ancient as they used to be, the world's customs are declining," but rather the widespread "daily life is declining." The poor are even poorer; those who "could still manage" in the past have all become poor. In the context of the bankruptcy of agriculture and the accelerated collapse of the economy in rural areas, closures, layoffs, and unemployment have formed widespread poverty. Ordinary people, because of "lack of means to survive," have no choice but to seek other ways out and "go down the wrong path." Finally, they "commit crimes" and "disrupt public order."

Therefore, this state of increase can absolutely not be stopped simply by increasing police force. In other words, if we do not think about improving the people's lives from this fundamental problem, then not only will we absolutely not eliminate this phenomenon, but on the contrary, it will only increase. So where do we start to improve the lives of ordinary people? In today's world, there is no "utopia" with no unemployment and very few crimes. May I ask, what path do we take to leave?

Small Memories of an Ancient City

— Luye

One year, I lingered in an ancient city. Now let me write a little bit of a memory here.

This ancient city, so I am not unfamiliar, customs and practices and simple folk, I also know and understand a little bit of; The scenery of the ancient city is also unique and interesting. If you want me to tell you the historical changes passed down from those ancient cities, I can also tell you. But this, someone has already taken as a historical record and notes of the information, and I can not write all the legends of the ancient city, and one by one the history and anecdotes. Here, let me first describe a little of the scenery of the ancient city.

On the city walls, there is not a single purple wild flower to decorate it, nor is there a single stem of foxtail grass or dandelion growing alone; In the past, there were also one or two gray soldiers on the city walls, dozing in the autumn sun, with their gun barrels facing the sky and their knees touching their knees, their military caps were pulled down low, and not even their mouths could be seen there. Interesting wild children, inserting a thin bamboo branch between their knees, the dry leaves rustling in the autumn wind; There are also some whose backs are painted with a large turtle, which seems to be slowly crawling on its back when viewed from a distance. When lonely, leaning on the railing in the small building and looking out, a knowing smile, often spreading on the corners of the mouth and eyebrows, can relieve some boredom. And this lonely, picturesque scenery, further increases the gray oldness of the ancient city!

Secondly, is the Drum Tower, in the ancient city, although is a feature, but it is not an original creation. And this drum tower, like others, is not worth investigating the details, can it be said that it can be distinguished how many years the drum tower has been? And the mythological legends are difficult to convince people, but in the ancient city there is a drum tower, which is ultimately the original color of this ancient city, we can know it without saying it. And the Drum Tower, to the wandering sons, who are wandering around in different places, has a little comfort, and also has a sad feeling. If one sleeps alone on the bed in the middle of the night, sticking to the wall and listening to the night watchman in the small alley, coughing with each step, has already accurately found which stone block is high and which stone is low, walking and knocking on the bamboo clapper, stopping at the bottom of the building, as usual, he is preparing to sleep stealthily here for a while. At this time, I can think of a small-mouthed lantern, quietly placed next to the bamboo clapper, illuminating a small square of the ground, and the sleepy face of the old night watchman.

At this moment, the big clock on the Drum Tower is striking, I can gently count them carefully: one, two, three, ... thinking, in this night without a big moon, where is there another fire, in the fire will be buried how many lives? I don't know how many wandering hearts have been pierced; this is not a schadenfreude psychology, but I, also feel that the night is long, boundless............

Is it really schadenfreude? However, this, can also make people suddenly miss each other, comforting the lonely heart of the solitary guest, in this night, can have dreams of the ancient city, absurd, magical and interesting, in the dream, one is almost invincible, can forget the hardship of being a guest, the heart from then on contains a kind of blind ambition for the times, this, the Drum Tower is given to people warmth.

In addition, gray sand is also a feature of the ancient city. On a windy day, the sky roads, the roofs are full of gray sand flying in a hazy way: on this day, in the evening when leaving work and rushing home, one can no longer see the person opposite. On the road, there is only a clang of the rickshaw puller's bells, seemingly ringing in the ears, looking back in the gray sand vague can see slightly red lanterns shuttling on the road. In the big wind, one cannot open one's mouth to speak loudly, as soon as one opens one's mouth, the gray sand drills into one's mouth, it is full, one can only close one's mouth tightly, bow one's head and walk, one's pace also hastens to rush home, one's face is covered with a thick layer of gray dust, only a pair of black eyes and a mouth are left, which can be seen in rotation. If you use

Page 20

Fingers cock the nostrils, have long been filled with gray earth, so, I can only smile bitterly.

But on a torrential rainy day, one can only run barefoot on the muddy road, and one must always be careful not to fall into the small mud edges of the empty streets.

In the ancient city, only the above-mentioned scenery can give me long-lasting memories.

Song of the Night

— Xin Er

(I) Dream

Moving to Jiangwan, a semi-rural area, I wanted to refresh my life, hoping to sort out the mess, the tangled feelings like a nightmare, next to the quiet and beautiful countryside. And perhaps I could purify my mind and write something. However, the countryside is quiet, but it is as if the old is always feeling somewhat lost; uneasiness and worries in the lonely black house, even more shadowy flashes!

For several years, what has made me tremble the most, what has been the most unbearable is: all night, as soon as I close my eyelids, I fall into a dream, at first it makes people feel more uneasy nostalgia, but gradually, it is just like dust blown by the wind, a mess of dreams. Waking up, I just feel dizzy and swollen, thinking of the life of cracking the whip and brandishing the claws, just at a loss, just like a lost child, confused and unable to distinguish. Recalling the clear and determined spirit of waking up from a sweet dream in the past, I shed tears. How can I struggle? Many people teach me to be quiet, to use my brain less, to take medicine, and not to be overly excited or sad; however, these are all very far away from me. These are all good friends of another kind of people. I can only groan far away under the iron hooves of life.

Ahead is a long journey! How will I, like a disabled traveler, get through it! This wounded traveler!

(II) Insomnia

However, the dreams only intensify. For a whole year now, I can't remember the appearance of the dream... Opening my eyes, even if I recall for half a day, I just can't support my dizzy head and fall down. Ah, will I never have a time to wake up from a dream! Closely following, disillusionment, the fantasy of escaping reality, gently floats up. Thus, during the day, fantasy and dreams also form a pitch-black mass. Thus, insomnia is sucking the blood that is about to dry up!

A dark night, a small, messy house. A dog is barking in the distance, the night wind carries the sound, passing into the silent window: the sound of the battle between life and death—I consciously tremble like this. I can't control my terrifying wailing and try my best to think! How can I shake up the life that is heading towards destruction! However, tired, confused, with anger wrapped around my body, tossing and turning, panting, opening my eyelids, countless black spots flash in front of me, I simply turn on the electric light, silence, desolation, sadness, I can only collapse, and still turn off the electric light. Closing my eyes, I can't control the thoughts that are even more chaotic like waves crashing. I regret that I shouldn't have, not silently let it pass.

"The past, but I can't get through it!" Another burst of burning pain.

Life is like smoke, not worth a few cents, like a chaotic dream! However, life must eventually go on, and before life, is an endless sea! Insomnia, chewing on me, I can only be like a dying worm. ...

(III) Song of the Night

Only in extreme fatigue, at the peak of confusion, when turning around from the tip, do I get a half-thread of quiet rest. And the song of the night, leaking in from the half-open window, makes me somewhat relieved to listen attentively.

Listen, this midnight song of Jiangwan! Although it is very ordinary.

Often it is the rhythmic sound of horseshoes hitting the cement, clattering, deeper and more powerful than the sound of frogs, it is the heavy footsteps of the traveling camel in this desert, doubly touching the heart of the traveler waiting to move forward, and making me seem to be slightly awake. From high to low to far away, and vaguely, disappearing so beautifully memorable; but just as I am finding the tail sound that seems to leave infinite aftertaste, the fresher and more powerful clattering footsteps surge up behind, faintly like the sound of war horses leaping on the battlefield. It makes me suddenly wake up and calmly open my eyes.

Ah, I breathed a sweet breath! It turned out that the slanting moon at the window was faintly beautiful and clear, my mind was refreshed, walking close to the window, I distinguished it! Is this the time for the grooms to let the horses go? That is the horse's feet moving forward! The dark night is about to end! Just as I was in doubt, a heroic singing sound came from afar, quickly, as if urging people under the window. Intermittently, it is all the country people who are carrying heavy burdens and going to the city, that hard, strong, and energetic labor song, deeply immersing into my empty heart.

Laughter

— Qin Jian

— A laugh a day, Keeps the doctor away. ("Laugh once a day, tell the doctor to get lost.")

An American wealthy businessman-type old gentleman, using a gentlemanly polite, unhurried tone, gently patted me on the shoulder, trying his best to look extremely sincere and concerned, said to me:

"Hey, kid, you're young, it's the age to be energetic, why are you always so gloomy, with a mourning face! Foreigners say: "Laugh once a day, tell the doctor to get lost": that's why foreigners are all energetic and can do great things: young people should always smile—I myself often had bright smiles when I was young. Yes, young people should always smile, should make themselves happy, should be energetic..."

There are so many "shoulds"! From his special expression, I saw a kind of despicable false sincerity hidden under his wrinkled face, covered under his British gentleman-style court dress! This is less of an encouragement from an old man to a young man in life, and more like a cruel carnivore filthily mocking a defeated little sheep in the victory of violence and immorality! So, in order to repay a gentleman's excessive "kindness", I finally laughed! I exposed all my teeth, opened my mouth, and shook my lips like a spasm.

"God, you kid! You laugh so terribly!"

"Yes, sir, I am not familiar with laughter."

"When you were a child, you saw your mother's lovely face, you saw the stars in the sky, didn't you often laugh?"

"No, sir, in my childhood, I saw my mother being beaten half to death by my father, I saw the wind blowing and rain and snow falling non-stop in winter, I often cried! Crying like..."

"God! What is this? What is this? This..."

"What is this?" It's really seeing his mother's ghost! Dragging a twenty-five-year-old body (is the "lovely young generation"!), dragging a "life" that is as heavy as a garbage dump, being suppressed under people every day, so that I can't even breathe! As tired as a sick stray dog, still laugh?

When has the term "laughter" (maybe there really is such a thing in the world? Maybe there isn't?) ever existed in my life history? I dare not recall the past, and dare not imagine the future. Living day after day like a machine with strange sounds of friction, I live in the world day after day.

In dreams, in the infrequent meditation, I often think like this: maybe there was another kind of laughter when I was a child? But what kind of thing should this be? And now, growing up, being thrown into the lonely and helpless oil pot of life, and those smiles, like encountering the most violent bombs, are blown to pieces, destroyed beyond recognition, and disappeared.

Disappeared! That is a scar of life that can never be recovered; that is a scar of life that can never be repaired! There are so many people who tell me many "shoulds" in suffering, such as: young people "should" be happy and energetic, "should" laugh!

However, what life can allow you to choose is only "yes" and "no", not "should" and "should not". For example: wandering, hunger, hardship, fatigue... Can that long string of ominous words still be explained with "should" and "should not"?

"Laugh," I often say to myself, "it's the time to be young, young people should always laugh!"

However, in the end I can only terribly show my teeth, shake, spasm, and babble; I understand: under the suppression of a not-so-light life, I am always clumsy at laughing; and laughter is not willing to climb onto my lowly face.

Has anyone ever seen the southern sun shine on the snowy land of the northern country?

Silver Waves

— Ai Tu

I love Macau on the shore of the raging waves, not because it is the Monte Carlo of the East—a complex big gambling place. But I am affected by a fresh and beautiful demeanor that blends the Eastern and Western Hemispheres. That's right: I always miss her like this, just like missing an unopened bud.

When I returned south this time, I had to wander to the beach of Macau again.

In the evening, when the steamer sailed from Guangzhou to the port of Macau, we could look out from the cabin, the waves constantly floating on the vast sea, as if silver was floating and floating, and at the same time, I heard the usual violent sound of the waves, which was carried by the sea breeze. The mountain peaks on the isolated coast are hung with charming colored lights. This is different from Hong Kong, more silent, just like a maiden in boudoir.

When I arrived in Macau and stepped on the stone-paved road of the pier, I routinely saw many flower-like girls standing on it waiting for their friends to come up. The daughters of Monte Carlo in the East are romantic, although the retro-style ethical and religious ideas are also strongly prevailing in the South, but, look! They are jumping and laughing so warmly and lovely, just like the silver waves at night are high-spirited, sounding a majestic tune, floating with the melody of the sea breeze, plus the women's singing coming out of the tall hotels, it constitutes a new circle of music.

After wandering around the prosperous streets with friends for a night, we entered the only magnificent dance floor and watched the enthusiastic demeanor of the people in the South, which was fascinating. Late at night, we began to wander again on the vast, clean and quiet beach, on the Western Bay Road made of cement.

That's right, I will never interrupt, in Macau, no matter what day and night, when people are intoxicated in the fiery circle. A few of us, who are young wanderers who are restless at home, began to silently seek a little taste of life that is left over in the realm of poetry. Every day is like this, but what answer to life do we get in the end? It is still the same indifferent! I often curse this contradiction in my own heart. But, forget it! I am such a wandering person! I can't blame myself, just as the beautiful silver waves can't always be as charming as they are at night.

Wandering on the flat and clear beach, the pale yellow street lights cast shadows from the dense and lush evergreen tree leaves, swaying non-stop. In the dark circles, we always often see pairs of men and women's shadows floating so intimately. - That's right, the night in Western Bay is the holy land of love! However, we don't care, and don't sneak a look, just like the Indian Asans in yellow uniforms who guard the night on the streets, we don't look much and slip away. And our purpose is to come to the beach to see the beautiful silver waves!

The silver waves are spreading out on the vast sea. Our eyeballs move with each wave, yes, we can believe that it is the shadow of melted silver! However, when the silver waves roll from the sea to the land, after a rustling sound, we can't see any shadow at all, only the ground is so wet, like after a heavy rain.

The wind blowing from the sea is so cool! When our legs are a little sore, Macau has returned to a quiet sleeping village. At this time, we have to return silently again, to a simple home for wanderers.

Broadcasting

Song Introduction

Merchant Girl

Smoke shrouds the cold water and the moon shrouds the gauze. Mooring on the Qinhuai River near the tavern, the merchant girl does not know the hatred of national subjugation. Across the river, she still sings the Backyard Flower! The merchant's daughter is sixteen years old, with a budding flower pistil falling with wild geese. Jade red runs rampant through Zhangtai, and there are lively carriages and horses in front of Pingkang Gate. Backyard Flower, sung endlessly, weaving jade hands playing the pipa, the golden lamp on the book beam is hung high, the room is full of spring warmth and boundless joy. The bronze stage ticks and the night leaks long, the corner of the house shines with moonlight, regardless of whether the Zheng River is about to burst, let's stay at the merchant girl's house tonight!

Movies

Recent News of the New Era

— Zhong

There is a role of local tyrants and evil gentry in "Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside". After a long search, it was decided to borrow You Guangzhao from the Star Company to play the role. The fat man wearing a robe and putting on a mustache is very funny.

"Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside" is a sound-on-film singing giant film. After working hard day and night, more than half of it has been filmed. Last night, the filmed film was previewed, and the light, sound, and acting skills were said to have amazing results.

Mr. Wang Tang Jie Xiao A Yuan Huang Naishuang went to Baidai Company yesterday at the invitation of the company to record "Singing Yangko" records. It is said that the work went smoothly and the results were gratifying. It is expected that the record will be popular throughout the country after its release.

Xiao Chen Cao Xuesong has put down his pen for a long time. Recently, he wrote a long novel on a whim in addition to filming, entitled "Two Orphans at the End of the World", which is 50,000 words long. It is said that it will be published in installments in the Women's Monthly starting from this month.

Newcomer Introduction

— Qingyun

Zhang Wen, a nineteen-year-old girl, has youth and energetic spirit, medium length, a healthy and beautiful physique,嘉寳-style long, unpermed hair like dark clouds, flexible eyes... Everything contains the conditions for the beauty of a modern girl. Friends, I tell you, she is the first one admitted among the hundreds of girls who applied for actresses in the spring of 1935 by Yihua Company, and she is also one of the most promising newcomers in the 1935 film industry.

She was originally from Jiaxing and lived in Hangzhou Municipal Middle School for several years. Therefore, she can read newspapers and write ordinary letters and articles. Because of her usual love for the emerging art of film, she broke through the fence built by her parents' corrupt ideas that she was not allowed to be a film actress, and came to her sister's house in Shanghai alone with a hopeful heart. Finally, her ideal was realized. In the chance encounter of Yihua's recruitment of actresses, under her artistic cultivation and all the conditions suitable for the screen, she became a member of the basic actresses of Yihua Company.

Although her ideal has been achieved, when her parents heard that she had entered the film industry, under the old thought that "actors are not good things at all", they believed that their daughter's entry into the film industry was a disgrace to the family, so they implemented their first step to force her to withdraw from the film industry by not providing living expenses. If she still stubbornly persists, then

However, Miss Zhang, who loves the emerging art of film very much, is willing to sacrifice everything to be a loyal warrior of film culture. In "At the Beginning of Man", she has already realized her ambition to appear on the screen, playing a "boat girl". Although there are not many shots, she performed well. Now, in the sound film "Storm", which is about to be released, she plays a female nurse. In the sound film "Hero of the Times" directed by Ying Yunwei, she plays the sister of a poor middle-aged man. We predict that judging from her spirit of striving for progress, she will never disappoint us.
